# Normative Rule Traceability — Ade

> **Status:** Living architectural document. Regenerated by `/traceability`; not hand-edited.
> Per-project instance of `~/.claude/methodology/templates/traceability.md`.

> 176 rules in `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` at HEAD (`928c2be`).
> 32 CI scripts under `ci/ci_check_*.sh`.
> Source of truth: `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` (canonical, append-only).
> **Refresh note (HEAD `928c2be`, PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE full close).**
> The proposal-procedures-decode cluster (PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE, 2 slices
> `70bc85b` PP-S1 → `928c2be` PP-S2) is now **fully closed at HEAD `928c2be`**.
> All six mechanical acceptance criteria CE-PP-1..CE-PP-6 are green in CI; no
> deferred half (unlike PHASE4-N-E). This is the first cluster since OQ5 to
> **add a new registry rule and a new CI script**: registry **175 → 176** (+1
> `DC-LEDGER-11`), CI **31 → 32** (+1 `ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh`,
> the 5-check mechanical guard on the closure). Family counts at HEAD `928c2be`:
> T: 29, DC: **65** (was 64, +1 for `DC-LEDGER-11`), CN: 69, OP: 7, RO: 6 —
> total **176**. The new rule `DC-LEDGER-11` (`status = "enforced"`,
> `introduced_in = "PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE"`) records that
> `proposal_procedures` MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the
> authoritative Conway tx-body shape: `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is
> typed `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` (was `Option<Vec<u8>>`), decoded
> through the single closed entry point `decode_proposal_procedures` that
> rejects unknown `gov_action` tags, structural failures, empty sets, and
> trailing garbage deterministically; the typed form re-encodes byte-identically
> (`PreservedCbor`) for every well-formed Conway tx body. The decoder reuses
> the existing closed `GovAction` enum (preserving the `DC-LEDGER-10`
> `UpdateCommittee` discriminant — the structured `{removed, added, threshold}`
> with `StakeCredential` cold members survives this decode) and the existing
> opaque `Anchor` struct. **Bidirectional cross_ref:** `DC-LEDGER-11.cross_ref
> = ["DC-LEDGER-10"]` and `DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` gains `DC-LEDGER-11` —
> bidirectional, pairing the credential-discriminant rule with its downstream
> tx-body-grammar rule. The new CI script
> `ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` (anchored on `DC-LEDGER-11` in
> its header comment) FAILs CI on any of five mechanical guards: (1)
> `ade_types::conway::governance` no longer defines the closed
> `ProposalProcedure` struct with all four fields (`deposit`, `return_addr`,
> `gov_action`, `anchor`); (2) `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` reverts from
> `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` to `Option<Vec<u8>>` (the prior opaque
> form); (3) the codec module `ade_codec::conway::governance` ceases to exist
> or stops exporting `decode_proposal_procedures` + `encode_proposal_procedures`;
> (4) the Conway tx-body codec at key 20 reverts to the prior
> `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through instead of the typed
> decoder/encoder; (5) any `ProposalProcedure {` struct-literal construction
> appears outside the sanctioned synthesis sites (the decoder itself in
> `ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs`, the GREEN harness under
> `ade_testkit/`, `crates/*/tests/`, and `#[cfg(test)]` inline test blocks —
> production callers MUST go through `decode_proposal_procedures`). **Test
> growth: +21 across PP-S1 + PP-S2** — 14 unit tests (in
> `ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` inline `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` —
> seven `roundtrip_*` tests covering every `GovAction` variant +
> `roundtrip_multi_procedure` + four `rejects_*` adversarial tests +
> `rejects_invalid_stake_credential_in_update_committee` +
> `update_committee_keeps_stake_credential_discriminant`), 3 integration
> tests in `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_tx_body_proposal_procedures.rs`
> (the typed key-20 path round-trips through `ConwayTxBody`; `None` skips
> key 20 entirely; sub-decoder and body decoder agree byte-for-byte), and 4
> corpus tests in `crates/ade_testkit/tests/proposal_procedures_corpus_replay.rs`
> driven by the canonical synthetic corpus + replay harness at
> `crates/ade_testkit/src/governance/proposal_procedures_replay.rs`
> (`canonical_corpus_decodes_to_expected_shape`,
> `canonical_corpus_round_trips_byte_identical`,
> `canonical_corpus_covers_all_gov_action_variants`,
> `canonical_corpus_includes_update_committee_discriminant_case`). All 21
> confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `928c2be`. **Type
> change:** `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` field type went `Option<Vec<u8>>`
> → `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>`. Approximately ten test files referenced
> the field with the old `Some(vec![0x80])` opaque placeholder; per OQ-8 they
> were converted to `None` where they did not need actual data — only two
> required an actual update (the rest already used `None`). One new canonical
> type added (`ProposalProcedure`) — captured in the parallel CODEMAP refresh.
> **Cluster archival:** `docs/clusters/PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE/` was
> `git mv`'d to `docs/clusters/completed/PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE/`; all 3
> files (`cluster.md` + `PP-S1.md` + `PP-S2.md`) now live under `completed/`.
> The only directory left under active `docs/clusters/` is the carried
> `PHASE4-N-B/` cross-reference stray (unchanged). **Open obligations
> recorded on `DC-LEDGER-11.open_obligation` (NOT regressions; deferred by
> cluster scope decisions):** OQ-1 — `voting_procedures` (tx body key 19)
> closure is the natural sibling cluster (same opaque-bytes shape, same
> pressure, deliberately deferred); this rule does NOT cover it. OQ-2/OQ-3
> — `ParameterChange.update` and `NewConstitution.raw` nested opacities are
> likewise deferred; they are future `strengthened_in` candidates if/when
> those sub-grammars are closed. OQ-4 — typed `RewardAccount` for
> `proposal_procedure.return_addr` is a separate fidelity decision. The
> constitution-coverage gate is expected to PASS at 176 entries (registry
> parses cleanly: `grep -c '^\[\[rules\]\]'` returns 176, no `status =
> "deprecated"` entries). **`DC-LEDGER-10` strengthening cross-check:** the
> rule stays `status = "enforced"`; `strengthened_in` is unchanged (this
> cluster pairs via `cross_ref`, not via a fifth strengthening — the
> `UpdateCommittee` discriminant survives the new typed decode without any
> new committee-surface code); `cross_ref` gains `DC-LEDGER-11` and is now
> `["T-DET-01", "T-ENC-03", "DC-LEDGER-08", "DC-LEDGER-09", "DC-LEDGER-11",
> "DC-TXV-05"]`; `DC-LEDGER-11.cross_ref = ["DC-LEDGER-10"]` — bidirectional.
> CODEMAP and HEAD_DELTAS are being **regenerated in parallel** with this
> TRACEABILITY refresh and are expected to catch up to HEAD `928c2be`:
> CODEMAP adds the `ProposalProcedure` canonical type + the
> `ade_codec::conway::governance` module + the GREEN
> `ade_testkit::governance::proposal_procedures_replay` harness; HEAD_DELTAS

> **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK (committee enactment wired at the epoch
> boundary) close** *strengthens* **two** existing rules **AGAIN** — `DC-EPOCH-01`
> (Conway governance timing / enactment atomicity) and `DC-LEDGER-10` (credential
> key/script discriminant fidelity) — **NO new rule, NO new CI script**. The
> registry total stays **173 rules** and the CI count stays **29 scripts** (the
> existing `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was *extended* —
> sections 7 + a write-back-wiring check — not added). This is the cluster that
> makes the previously-dormant committee-enactment effect **live**: committee
> enactment is now wired at the epoch boundary
> (`ade_ledger::governance::apply_committee_enactment`, called from
> `ade_ledger::rules`). A ratified `NoConfidence` action **dissolves the
> committee**; a ratified `UpdateCommittee` action **removes/adds discriminated
> cold members and sets the new quorum** (previously the committee was cloned
> unchanged, silently dropping ratified committee changes). `DC-EPOCH-01`
> (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`) gains the wired
> `apply_committee_enactment` Code surface, the
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` CI gate, and **four** new tests
> (`enact_noconfidence_dissolves_committee`,
> `enact_update_committee_applies_changes`,
> `committee_enactment_replays_byte_identical`,
> `epoch_boundary_ratified_noconfidence_dissolves_committee`); it stays
> `status = "partial"` because the governance-Plutus oracle is still deferred to
> CE-88. `DC-LEDGER-10` (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`):
> the discriminated committee credential now **survives the live enactment
> write-back** — `GovAction::UpdateCommittee` is structured (`{removed:
> BTreeSet<StakeCredential>, added: BTreeMap<StakeCredential,u64>, threshold}`,
> replacing opaque raw bytes), the snapshot-loader decode is fail-closed on an
> unknown credential tag, and the write-back path itself preserves the tag — not
> just the dormant type. Its `tests` array grows from 14 to **19** with five
> tests (`update_committee_decodes_removed_added_threshold`,
> `update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_members_distinct`,
> `update_committee_decode_rejects_malformed`,
> `update_committee_structured_fields_change_fingerprint`,
> `enact_update_committee_keyhash_scripthash_distinct`), all confirmed to exist as
> functions in the codebase at HEAD `3180e27`. The gate
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was extended (sections 7 +
> write-back-wiring check); `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (173
> entries). This close **resolves the prior OQ5 follow-up (d) write-back risk** as
> a now-live, discriminant-preserving enactment; the remaining `DC-LEDGER-10`
> follow-ups are only (e) the GREEN loader `mk_credential` older-helper unknown-tag
> default (contained to `ade_testkit`) and (b) the `shelley/cert.rs` unknown-cert
> zero-hash `KeyHash` placeholder. **Surfaced enforcement gap (unchanged class):**
> `DC-EPOCH-01`'s real-chain committee-transition oracle is **environment-blocked**
> (no local snapshot exhibits a committee change) — a genuine open obligation,
> reclassified per tier doctrine. See §A0000000000 (newest) and §G #30.
> **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY (committee-enactment write-back credential
> discriminant fidelity) close** *strengthens* the existing `DC-LEDGER-10` rule
> **AGAIN** (`strengthened_in = ["COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY", "DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY",
> "ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY"]`) — **NO new rule, NO new CI script**. The
> registry total stays **173 rules** and the CI count stays **29 scripts** (the
> existing `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was *extended* — a 6th
> check on the committee-enactment write-back surface — not added). It **resolves
> the prior OQ5 follow-up (d)** as a *preventive migration*:
> `EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` (`ade_ledger::governance`) is re-typed
> `Option<(Vec<Hash28>, Vec<(Hash28, u64)>)>` →
> `Option<(Vec<StakeCredential>, Vec<(StakeCredential, u64)>)>`, so when committee
> enactment (`UpdateCommittee`) is eventually wired it **cannot re-collapse the
> discriminated committee map on write-back**. The field stays **dormant** (`None`
> — `UpdateCommittee` enactment is still a no-op), so this is a structural
> guard-rail, not a behavioural change. `DC-LEDGER-10`'s `tests` array is extended
> from 13 to **14** with one enactment test
> (`enactment_committee_changes_keyhash_scripthash_distinct`, confirmed to exist as
> a function at `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs:584` during this refresh). The
> CI gate `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` defends the new surface
> (`EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` stays `StakeCredential`-typed);
> `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (173 entries). This close
> **resolves OQ5 follow-up (d)**; the remaining `DC-LEDGER-10` follow-ups are now
> only (e) the GREEN loader `mk_credential` unknown-tag default to `KeyHash`
> (contained to `ade_testkit`) and (b) the `shelley/cert.rs` unknown-cert zero-hash
> `KeyHash` placeholder. See §A000000000 (newest) and §G #29.
> **DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY (DRep-voter credential key/script discriminant fidelity)
> close** *strengthens* the existing `DC-LEDGER-10` rule **AGAIN**
> (`strengthened_in = ["COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY", "DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY"]`) — **NO new
> rule, NO new CI script**. The registry total stays **173 rules** and the CI count
> stays **29 scripts** (the existing `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh`

> the prior OQ5 follow-up (c): `GovActionState.drep_votes`
> (`ade_types::conway::governance`) is re-typed `Vec<(Hash28, Vote)>` →
> `Vec<(StakeCredential, Vote)>`, so the DRep-voter surface is now **discriminated**;
> `ade_ledger::governance`'s `lookup_stake` closure resolves DRep stake by **exact
> variant** (no key/script OR-fallback over identical bytes — a key-hash DRep and a
> script-hash DRep sharing 28 bytes do not cross-resolve); the fingerprint emits the
> DRep-vote discriminant via `fingerprint::write_credential_vote_list` (renamed from
> `write_committee_vote_list`, now serving committee + DRep); the GREEN snapshot
> loader's `parse_credential_vote_map` (renamed from `parse_committee_vote_map`)
> preserves the DRep tag. `spo_votes` stays `Hash28`-keyed by design (pools are
> always key-hash — a permanent non-goal). `DC-LEDGER-10`'s `tests` array is extended
> from 11 to **13** with two DRep tests
> (`drep_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve`,
> `drep_vote_discriminant_changes_fingerprint`), both confirmed to exist as functions
> at HEAD `62c9020`. The CI gate `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh`
> **PASSES at HEAD `62c9020`** (verified during this refresh: `PASS: DC-LEDGER-10
> credential discriminant is closed and faithful (incl. committee + DRep-vote
> surfaces)`, exit 0); `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` **PASSES** (173
> entries). This close **resolves OQ5 follow-up (c)**; the remaining `DC-LEDGER-10`
> follow-ups are (d) `EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` still bare `Hash28` but
> **dormant** (`UpdateCommittee` enactment is a no-op) — must migrate to
> `StakeCredential` before committee enactment; (e) the GREEN loader `mk_credential`
> unknown-tag default to `KeyHash` (contained to `ade_testkit`); and (b) the
> `shelley/cert.rs` unknown-cert zero-hash `KeyHash` placeholder. See §A00000000
> (newest) and §G #28.
> **COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY (committee credential key/script discriminant
> fidelity) close** *strengthens* the existing `DC-LEDGER-10` rule
> (`strengthened_in += COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY`) — **NO new rule**; the registry
> total stays **173 rules** and the CI count stays **29 scripts** (the existing
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` was *extended*, not added). It
> closes the committee-credential surface that was OQ5's declared follow-up (a):
> `ConwayGovState.committee` (`ade_ledger::state`) and
> `GovActionState.committee_votes` (`ade_types::conway::governance`) are now keyed
> on / carry the discriminated `StakeCredential` rather than a bare `Hash28`;
> `governance::evaluate_ratification` / `check_ratification` resolve a committee
> vote by **full-credential equality** (no `.hash()` on the committee path), so a
> hot/cold authorization cannot cross-resolve a key-hash vote onto a script-hash
> member; the canonical fingerprint emits the committee discriminant via the new
> `fingerprint::write_committee_vote_list` (committee votes) and
> `write_stake_credential` (the committee map); the GREEN snapshot loader's
> `parse_committee_state` + `parse_committee_vote_map` preserve the committee tag.
> `DC-LEDGER-10`'s `tests` array is extended from 8 to **11** with three committee
> tests (`committee_keyhash_scripthash_do_not_cross_resolve`,
> `committee_keyhash_scripthash_same_bytes_distinct`,
> `committee_discriminant_changes_fingerprint`), all confirmed to exist as
> functions at HEAD `2aeea16`. The CI gate
> `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` **PASSES at HEAD `2aeea16`**
> (verified during this refresh: `PASS: DC-LEDGER-10 credential discriminant is
> closed and faithful (incl. committee surface)`, exit 0);
> `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` **PASSES** (173 entries). This close
> resolves OQ5 follow-up (a) and surfaces three new bounded follow-ups recorded in
> `DC-LEDGER-10`'s `open_obligation`: (c) DRep-vote discrimination —
> `governance.rs` `lookup_stake` still does a key/script OR-fallback over identical
> bytes for `drep_votes` (the recommended next discriminant cluster); (d)
> `EnactmentEffects.committee_changes` is still bare `Hash28` but **dormant**
> (`UpdateCommittee` enactment is a no-op) — it MUST be migrated to
> `StakeCredential` before committee enactment is implemented; (e) the GREEN loader
> `mk_credential` defaults an unknown tag to `KeyHash` (contained to `ade_testkit`,
> cannot reach the node binary). See §A0000000 (newest) and §G #25, #26, #27.
> **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY (credential key/script discriminant fidelity) close**

> UMap/VState — epoch-576/boundary snapshots absent locally, recoverable from the

> stays hash-level — the committee member/vote types were out of OQ5 scope while
> `committee_hot_keys` was in (per-cluster security review WARN/MEDIUM); (b) the
> `shelley/cert.rs` unknown-cert zero-hash `KeyHash` placeholder (pre-existing,
> ignored by `apply_cert`) should be closed when the Shelley cert grammar is
> closed (WARN/LOW). This close also **resolves the prior §G #21 OQ-5 declared
> follow-up** — OQ-5 has graduated from a declared follow-up on `DC-LEDGER-09`

> follow-up**, and `status = "partial"` honestly reflects it — it is the **one

> §H value-conservation completeness gap** (deposit/refund/withdrawal accounting now
> in scope). PHASE4-B2 (tx validity agreement) added the 5-rule `DC-TXV-01..05`

> (new `ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh`). PHASE4-B1 (full block
> validity agreement) close added the 6-rule `DC-VAL-*` sub-family.

---

## Conventions

- **Source of rules.** The canonical, append-only source is the invariant
  registry at `.idd-config.json` `invariant_registry`
  (`docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml`). The registry was renamed from
  `constitution_registry.toml` in the post-Phase-4-N-D IDD-canonicalization
  delta (`ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` was repointed in `39865f6`).
  Every `[[rules]]` entry whose `status` is not explicitly retired appears
  below. None are deprecated at HEAD.
- **Rule IDs** are stable across regenerations and immutable per
  registry doctrine. They are reproduced exactly as the registry holds them.
- **Families.** The registry groups rules under five family-letter
  prefixes:

  | Prefix | Family |
  |---|---|
  | `T-` | True invariants (project constitution §2) |
  | `DC-` | Derived Cardano compatibility invariants (§3) |
  | `CN-` | Classification-table invariants (`classification_table.md`) |
  | `RO-` | Release obligations (§4a) |
  | `OP-` | Operational invariants (§4b) |

  Within each family, level-3 sub-headings hold one rule each. The
  sub-section ID *is* the rule ID. Within a family, ordering follows
  the registry file order. The `DC-CONS-*` sub-family (8 rules
  introduced by PHASE4-N-B) appears at the end of the `DC-` section in
  registry file order.
- **Four-cell contract.** Every rule carries the canonical four-row table:
  Source, Requirement, Code, Tests, CI. Where the registry has populated
  `code_locus`, `tests`, `ci_script`, those fields drive the row. A row
  marked `_(no enforcement found — gap)_` corresponds to a registry
  entry whose `status` is `declared` (no enforcement promised) or to a
  partial entry that has not yet pointed at a code/test/CI artifact.
- **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY close (credential key/script discriminant fidelity).**
  This cluster introduced **1 new `DC-LEDGER-10` rule** (`status = "enforced"`) and
  back-referenced it bidirectionally from `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-03`, `DC-LEDGER-08`,
  `DC-LEDGER-09`, `DC-TXV-05`. `DC-LEDGER-10` *strengthens* `T-DET-01` (the
  discriminated `StakeCredential`/`ConwayGovState` representation is a deliberate,
  oracle-confirmable cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration) and `T-ENC-03`
  (the credential decoders round-trip the key/script discriminant rather than
  erasing it), and *relates* `DC-LEDGER-08`/`DC-LEDGER-09` (the cert-state and
  gov-state these rules accumulate are now keyed on the discriminated credential)
  and `DC-TXV-05` (required-signer / witness closure resolves credentials by
  discriminated identity). The new authority surface is
  `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`StakeCredential` closed 2-variant enum
  `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` + `hash()` accessor — replaces the tuple-struct
  `StakeCredential(Hash28)`), `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` +
  `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_stake_credential` preserves the
  tag, rejects unknown), `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`ConwayGovState`
  re-keyed to `StakeCredential`), `gov_cert.rs`/`governance.rs`/`cert_classify.rs`/
  `rules.rs` (`cred.hash()` boundary adapter for the `Hash28`-keyed stake
  snapshot), and `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`write_stake_credential`
  emits discriminant+hash; gov-map writers use it; the stake-snapshot writer stays
  `write_hash28` by design). The GREEN testkit
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/harness/snapshot_loader.rs` preserves the tag in its
  gov-map + DRep-reg parses. **One new CI script landed** —
  `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (anchored on `DC-LEDGER-10`),
  bringing the total to **29**. OQ5 carries one environment-blocked open
  obligation (the real-chain discriminated-credential agreement vs cardano-node's
  `Credential`-keyed UMap/VState, reclassified per tier doctrine), declared
  non-goals (withdrawal/required-signer/address credential discriminant, the
  `Hash28`-keyed stake-distribution snapshot, the Byron credential surface), and
  two declared per-cluster-security-review follow-ups bounded to those non-goal
  surfaces (committee member/vote discrimination; the Shelley unknown-cert
  zero-hash placeholder). This close also **resolves the prior OQ-5 declared
  follow-up on `DC-LEDGER-09`** — OQ-5 graduates into the enforced `DC-LEDGER-10`.
  See §A000000 and §G #21, #23.
- **PHASE4-B5 close (Conway governance-certificate accumulation authority).**
  Cluster PHASE4-B5 introduced **1 new `DC-LEDGER-09` rule** (`status = "enforced"`)
  and **strengthened `DC-LEDGER-08`** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B5`): B5 makes the
  governance certs B4 owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` **applied** rather than
  observed-and-dropped, retiring `DC-LEDGER-08`'s "routed out-of-mutation-scope"
  disposition for governance certs. The new authority surface is
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs` (`apply_conway_gov_cert`, native gov dispatch
  total over 18 tags), `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`GovCertEnv` +
  `LedgerState::gov_cert_env()` fail-fast constructor),
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams.drep_activity`),
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`ValidationEnvironmentError::{MissingDRepActivityParam,
  DRepActivityOverflow}`), `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs`
  (`accumulate_tx_certs` / `process_block_certificates` thread
  `Option<ConwayGovState>`, apply the gov half, carry `gov_state` forward through
  `apply_block` — replaces the B4 observe-and-drop), and
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (gov-state + `drep_activity` fingerprint
  surface — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable migration making `ConwayGovState` a
  deterministic function of boundary-base + replayed block-stream cert effects).
  **One new CI script landed** — `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh`
  (anchored on `DC-LEDGER-09`), bringing the total to **28**. The B5 close also
  **RESOLVES the prior §G #18 bidirectional-cross_ref defect** (the gate now PASSES
  at HEAD `651adc9`, 172 entries — verified during this refresh). B5 carries one
  environment-blocked open obligation (the real epoch-576 VState oracle, reclassified
  per tier doctrine) and two declared separable follow-ups (OQ-3 committee-membership
  tx-validity gate; OQ-5 credential key/script discriminant collapse). See §A00000
  and §G #18–#21.
- **PHASE4-B2 close (tx validity agreement).** Cluster PHASE4-B2
  (single-transaction validity; the body authority's per-tx half) introduced
  **5 new `DC-TXV-*` rules** (`DC-TXV-01..05`, all `enforced`), flipped
  **`DC-MEM-01` and `DC-MEM-02`** `declared -> enforced` (the mempool gained a
  real `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/` BLUE module), and strengthened **6
  pre-existing rules** by appending `PHASE4-B2` to `strengthened_in`:
  `DC-LEDGER-05` and `CN-LEDGER-09` (Conway vkey-witness binding — fail-closed
  Ed25519 coverage over the preserved body hash), `DC-VAL-06` (wrong-size
  vkey/sig now `MalformedWitnessField` on the tx path; unresolvable inputs
  fail-fast), `DC-LEDGER-02` (GREEN no-false-accept tx adversarial corpus),
  `T-ENC-01` (`tx_id` lifted byte-for-byte from the body slice, never
  re-encoded), and `T-DET-01` (tx verdict-surface replay over the Conway-576
  corpus). The new authority surface is `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`
  (closed `TxValidityVerdict`/`TxRejectClass`/`TxValidityError`,
  `transition.rs` phase-1 ∧ phase-2 composition with phase-1-first fail-fast,
  `required_signers.rs` closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enumeration over
  every signer source, `witness.rs` fail-closed coverage over the preserved
  body hash, `phase1.rs` decode + state-backed checks) and the mempool BLUE
  module `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/{admit,policy}.rs` (closed `AdmitOutcome`
  / `OrderPolicy`; admission verdict equals `tx_validity` verdict; overload
  policy never changes a verdict). The GREEN corpus harnesses live at
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/`. **No new CI script landed in B2** —
  every `DC-TXV-*` / `DC-MEM-*` rule carries
  `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (extended in B2 to scan
  `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/` and `ade_ledger/src/mempool/` for closed
  structured verdicts/outcomes) plus its test surface. The same close
  **populated the previously-empty `ci_script`** on every enforced `DC-CONS-*`
  and `DC-VAL-*` rule with `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`, which is what
  flips `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` from FAIL to **PASS** at HEAD
  (the coverage gate requires a non-empty `ci_script` on every `enforced`
  entry). The earlier "documented deposit/refund value-conservation gap" — the
  Conway state-backed coin-conservation check conservatively skipping txs
  carrying certificates or withdrawals — was **CLOSED in PHASE4-B3-S4**. The
  cert/withdrawal early-out was removed from
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` (the
  source comment at the function header explicitly records "PHASE4-B3-S4
  removed the deposit/withdrawal early-out that was the cluster's known
  false-accept path"); the full preservation-of-value equation
  (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee + donation + new_deposits`)
  now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs, with deposit amounts
  sourced canonically via `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-07`. See §H (kept for
  provenance) and `T-CONSERV-01` / `CN-LEDGER-07`.
- **PHASE4-B1 close (full block validity agreement).** Cluster PHASE4-B1
  (block validity agreement; dependency root for B2/B3) introduced **6 new
  `DC-VAL-*` rules** (`DC-VAL-01..06`, all `enforced`) and strengthened **6
  pre-existing rules** by appending `PHASE4-B1` to `strengthened_in` and wiring
  the new block-validity surface: `T-DET-01` (verdict-surface replay over the
  Conway-576 positive corpus), `DC-CRYPTO-01` (Praos single-VRF input +
  leader/nonce range extension, op-cert-signable fix), `DC-CONSENSUS-02`
  (`LedgerView` projection), `DC-LEDGER-02` (GREEN no-false-accept adversarial

  and `CN-EPOCH-01` (`consensus_view` projection). The new authority surface is

  `crates/ade_ledger/src/{consensus_input_extract,consensus_view}.rs` (pure

  **No new CI script landed in B1** — every `DC-VAL-*` rule carries an empty

  The earlier "documented Conway body-witness verification gap" (recorded in
  `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` and the corresponding
  README) was **CLOSED in PHASE4-B2-S1 (CE-B2-1)**: per-tx Ed25519 vkey-witness
  verification over the preserved body hash is wired into the body path via
  `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs::verify_required_witnesses`
  (L78), called from `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs:258` and `:342` via
  `verify_conway_witness_closure`. The gap is no longer carried forward; see
  `DC-LEDGER-05` / `CN-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05` for the closed surface.
- **PHASE4-N-B close (consensus runtime).** Cluster N-B (Praos consensus

- **Phase 4 N-A CI closure (PHASE4-N-A close).** Cluster N-A (Ouroboros

- **Phase 4 N-D CI closure (`78da6c9`).** Three CI scripts —
  `ci/ci_check_chaindb_contract.sh`, `ci/ci_check_recovery_contract.sh`,
  `ci/ci_check_chaindb_crash_safety.sh` — flipped nine
  recovery/storage rules `declared → enforced`: `T-REC-01`, `T-REC-02`,
  `DC-STORE-01`, `DC-STORE-02`, `DC-STORE-03`, `DC-STORE-05`,
  `CN-STORE-03`, `CN-STORE-04`, `CN-STORE-05`. `DC-STORE-04` remains
  `declared` by design — see §B for the Tier 5 divergence note.
- **CI script BLUE scope (closed at `5b70bee`).** All seven BLUE-scoped
  CI scripts hard-code the full six-crate BLUE list `{ade_codec,
  ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` declared
  by `.idd-config.json` plus the 9 BLUE `ade_network` submodule paths.
  No `_(scope gap)_` markers remain.

---

## T — True Invariants (Project Constitution §2)

### `T-DET-01`: Same canonical inputs → same authoritative bytes

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2; `comparison_surface_contract.md` (Byte Authority Model §3). PHASE4-B5 adds `DC-LEDGER-09` to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the `ConwayGovState` fingerprint migration — gov state as a deterministic function of boundary-base + replayed block-stream cert effects rather than a frozen snapshot — is a deliberate, oracle-confirmable `T-DET-01` surface. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the discriminated `StakeCredential` makes `CertState`/`ConwayGovState` key on the key/script discriminant and `fingerprint::write_stake_credential` serializes it, so two states differing only in a credential's tag fingerprint differently — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration. |
| **Requirement** | Replaying the same canonical inputs against the same prior state must yield byte-identical authoritative outputs. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`apply_block*` family), `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (canonical per-component state hash; PHASE4-B3 adds a Conway-gated deposit-param fold to `fingerprint_pparams` — non-Conway states fingerprint byte-identically, Conway states fold in the canonical deposit params, see `DC-TXV-07`); plus PHASE4-N-B consensus surface — `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/encoding.rs` (canonical state encoding with deterministic op-cert counter map iteration) and `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/chain_selector.rs` (GREEN orchestrator that drives BLUE transitions deterministically); plus PHASE4-B1 verdict-surface replay — `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/replay.rs` (GREEN harness replaying `block_validity` over the 14-block Conway-576 positive corpus); plus PHASE4-B2 tx verdict-surface replay — `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/` (GREEN harness `replay_tx_validity` driving the BLUE `tx_validity` over every extracted Conway-576 corpus tx twice, surfaces byte-identical). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/ledger_determinism.rs::apply_block_deterministic`; per-era `byron_determinism`, `shelley_determinism`, `allegra_determinism`, `mary_determinism`, `alonzo_determinism`, `babbage_determinism`, `conway_determinism`; plus consensus subset closed via `crates/ade_testkit/tests/consensus_stream_replay.rs::{synthetic_session_replays_identically, synthetic_session_event_kinds_match_corpus, synthetic_session_final_state_matches_corpus, op_cert_regression_header_rejected_mid_stream}` (CE-N-B-5) and the canonical state-roundtrip battery `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_state_canonical_roundtrip.rs::{layout_is_stable, roundtrip_empty_state, roundtrip_genesis_state, roundtrip_populated_state, roundtrip_chain_event_all_variants, roundtrip_chain_selection_reject_all_variants, op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic}`; plus PHASE4-B1 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_positive_corpus.rs::verdict_stream_replays_identically` (the block-validity verdict surface replays byte-identically over the Conway-576 corpus); plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_positive_corpus.rs::tx_verdict_stream_replays_identically` (the tx-validity verdict surface replays byte-identically over the Conway-576 corpus); plus PHASE4-B3 `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::tests::{pparams_fingerprint_stable_for_non_conway, pparams_fingerprint_includes_conway_deposits_when_present}` (the Conway deposit-param fold is byte-identical for non-Conway states and stable when present). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` (BLUE forbidden patterns, all 6 BLUE crates), `ci/ci_check_ledger_determinism.sh` (replay equivalence), `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (PHASE4-N-B — no `#[non_exhaustive]`, no `Other`/`Unknown` open-tail variants, no owned `String` or `Box<dyn>` in `ade_core::consensus`). Strengthened for PHASE4-N-B, again for PHASE4-B1 (block-validity verdict-surface replay), and again for PHASE4-B2 (tx-validity verdict-surface replay; no new CI script — discharged by `tx_verdict_stream_replays_identically` plus the structural consensus gates, which now also scan `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/` and `ade_ledger/src/mempool/`). |

### `T-ENC-01`: Canonical encoding for persisted/hashed/transmitted data

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2. Strengthened by PHASE4-B1 (block body hash over preserved CBOR) and PHASE4-B2 (`tx_id` over preserved body slice). |
| **Requirement** | All persisted, hashed, or transmitted authoritative bytes use a single canonical encoding; hash-critical bytes are taken from the preserved wire segment, never re-encoded. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs` (`PreservedCbor<T>`, `pub(crate)` constructor); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (PHASE4-B1 — block body hash computed over the preserved CBOR segment bytes, never re-encoded); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (PHASE4-B2 — `decode_tx`: `tx_id = blake2b_256` of the body slice lifted byte-for-byte from the full tx CBOR, never a re-encode). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/...::preserved_wire_bytes_returned_exactly`; `crates/ade_ledger/...::altered_body_rejected_by_hash_binding`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::tx_id_uses_preserved_bytes`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_hash_uses_wire_bytes.sh` — scans all 6 BLUE crates `{ade_codec, ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` for `hash(canonical_*)` patterns. Status = `partial` (canonical-encoding surface not yet fully covered; the `tx_id`-preserved-bytes property is proven by test only). |

### `T-ENC-03`: Round-trip identity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, D-3. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): both era credential decoders preserve the key/script discriminant rather than erasing it, so `decode_stake_credential` round-trips the tag — `encode(decode(bytes)) == bytes` extends to the credential-type discriminant. |
| **Requirement** | For all valid encodings, `encode(decode(bytes)) == bytes`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs`; plus per-protocol codecs `crates/ade_network/src/codec/{handshake,n2c_handshake,chain_sync,block_fetch,tx_submission,keep_alive,peer_sharing,local_chain_sync,local_tx_submission,local_state_query,local_tx_monitor}.rs` (PHASE4-N-A S-A2). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/...::full_corpus_round_trip` — 10,500 contiguous blocks across 7 eras; per-protocol synthetic `codec::<proto>::tests::roundtrip_every_variant` across all 11 mini-protocols (S-A2); plus six real-capture corpora harvested from cardano-node 11.0.1 — `handshake_real_capture_corpus`, `chain_sync_real_capture_corpus`, `block_fetch_real_capture_corpus`, `keep_alive_real_capture_corpus`, `peer_sharing_real_capture_corpus` (preprod local), `n2c_handshake_real_capture_corpus::real_capture_round_trips_byte_identical`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_cbor_round_trip.sh` (block-corpus round-trip); `ci/ci_check_ce_n_a_5_proof.sh` (CE-N-A-5 condition 3 — real-capture round-trip across 6 captured mini-protocols). |

### `T-CORE-02`: Forbidden nondeterminism

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, D-2 through D-5. |
| **Requirement** | No wall-clock, unseeded randomness, floats, `HashMap`/`HashSet`/`IndexMap`, `tokio`, `async fn`, or nondeterministic collections may appear in BLUE code. |
| **Code** | All six BLUE crates carry `#![deny(unsafe_code)]`, `#![deny(clippy::unwrap_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::expect_used)]`, `#![deny(clippy::panic)]`, `#![deny(clippy::float_arithmetic)]` in `lib.rs`. PHASE4-N-B narrows further: `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/*` uses Rational arithmetic (e.g. `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/vrf_cert.rs`) and never f32/f64 — verified by `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`. |
| **Tests** | _(structural — enforced by lint + CI text scans)_; consensus-scoped Rational evidence in `crates/ade_core/tests/vrf_cert_threshold.rs::{taylor_exp_cmp_le_zero_x_returns_false, taylor_exp_cmp_le_x_equals_one_returns_true, taylor_exp_cmp_le_monotone_in_x, is_leader_determinism, is_leader_known_vector_matches_reference}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` — scans `{ade_codec, ade_types, ade_crypto, ade_core, ade_ledger, ade_plutus}` for `HashMap`, `HashSet`, `IndexMap`, `SystemTime`, `Instant`, `std::fs`, `std::net`, `tokio`, `async fn`, `f32`/`f64`, `anyhow`, `rand::thread_rng`, `thread::spawn`, plus `unsafe` outside an allowlist. PHASE4-N-B added `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh` — narrowly scans `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/` for `f32`/`f64` tokens, redundant with `forbidden_patterns` for `ade_core` but pinned to the consensus tree to anchor `DC-CONS-{07,08,09}`. |

Check 3 forbids raw CBOR decoding outside `ade_codec`, with `ade_plutus/src/evaluator.rs` allowlisted because `PlutusScript::from_cbor` is the named Plutus-script CBOR chokepoint. |

### `T-CONS-02`: Consensus must not depend on host nondeterminism

### `T-CONSERV-01`: UTxO and asset conservation

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, audit #13. |
| **Requirement** | UTxO and asset conservation must hold for every accepted transition, except for explicitly authorized mint/burn/rewards/treasury flows. |

| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/..::all_eras_replay_summary`, `byron_replay_all_1500`, `shelley_replay_all_1500`; plus PHASE4-B3 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_full.rs::{conway_conservation_full, conservation_early_out_removed}`, `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_adversarial.rs::{adversarial_imbalanced_via_deposit, adversarial_imbalanced_via_withdrawal, adversarial_no_false_accept}`, `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_positive_synthetic.rs::{synthetic_balanced_cert_withdrawal_txs_are_valid, synthetic_positive_verdict_stream_replays_byte_identical}`, and the real-corpus positive coverage `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_positive_corpus.rs::{all_corpus_txs_valid, corpus_tx_count_nonzero}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_differential_divergence.sh`; plus PHASE4-B3 `ci/ci_check_ledger_determinism.sh` (the cert/withdrawal-bearing conservation path now folds into the deterministic ledger surface). The full-equation accept/reject property has no dedicated conservation-corpus CI gate — proven by the named tests; see §G. |

### `T-CAUSAL-01`: No retroactive reinterpretation

### `DC-EPOCH-01`: Conway governance timing

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-CAUSAL-01`, `T-EPOCH-01`. **Strengthened by ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** (`strengthened_in += ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK`): committee enactment is now wired at the epoch boundary (previously the committee was cloned unchanged, silently dropping ratified committee changes). Stays `status = "partial"` — the governance-Plutus oracle is still deferred to CE-88. |
| **Requirement** | Proposals accumulate during the epoch; ratification and enactment are atomic at the epoch boundary; pulsing distributes DRep stake computation across the epoch. ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK makes the committee half of enactment atomic-at-boundary: a ratified `NoConfidence` dissolves the committee, a ratified `UpdateCommittee` removes/adds discriminated cold members and sets the new quorum — applied as a pure transition at the boundary, never mid-epoch. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs` (`enact_proposals`; **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** `apply_committee_enactment` — pure transition: `NoConfidence` dissolve + discriminated `UpdateCommittee` remove/add + quorum); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (epoch-boundary apply site — calls `apply_committee_enactment` on the ratified committee action, ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK-S2). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/..::conway_epoch_boundary_end_to_end`, `crates/ade_ledger/...::conway_governance_ratification_test`; plus **ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK** (4 new) `crates/ade_ledger/src/governance.rs::{enact_noconfidence_dissolves_committee, enact_update_committee_applies_changes, committee_enactment_replays_byte_identical}` (a ratified `NoConfidence` dissolves the committee; a ratified `UpdateCommittee` removes/adds the discriminated members and sets the quorum; committee enactment replays byte-identically) and `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::epoch_boundary_ratified_noconfidence_dissolves_committee` (the epoch-boundary apply site dissolves a committee on a ratified `NoConfidence`). All 4 confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `3180e27`. **+1 since `3d94c22` (commit `b9cfaf9`, real-chain oracle):** `crates/ade_testkit/tests/epoch_oracle_comparison.rs::committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` — drives the mainnet Conway 575/576 ledger-state snapshots (snapshot-gated; skips when corpus absent) through our ratification + enactment and asserts no-op write-back agreement: cardano-node enacted no committee change across the boundary, and `apply_committee_enactment` fabricates none. Reclassifies the prior environment-blocked no-op case to **reality-blocked** for the positive committee-CHANGE case (mainnet enacted no `UpdateCommittee`/`NoConfidence` in this range, so no snapshot pair has a committee delta to diff). Confirmed to exist as a function at HEAD `168ac02`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK — sections 7 + the write-back-wiring check defend the committee-enactment write-back surface; this is now `DC-EPOCH-01`'s `ci_script`). _(Surfaced enforcement gap, now narrower: the real-chain committee **no-op** agreement is now ORACLE-CONFIRMED at the mainnet Conway 575→576 boundary by `committee_oracle_mainnet_575_576_noop_agreement` (`crates/ade_testkit/tests/epoch_oracle_comparison.rs`, commit `b9cfaf9`) — our loader parses the 7-member `ScriptHash` interim committee exactly, and our ratification + enactment reproduces the epoch-576 committee with no spurious mutation. The positive committee-CHANGE case is **reality-blocked**, not environment-blocked (mainnet enacted no `UpdateCommittee`/`NoConfidence` in this range, so no snapshot pair exhibits a committee delta to diff). The governance-Plutus oracle (CE-88) is the other deferred half keeping the rule at `status = "partial"`. Recorded in the registry `authority_surface`; status stays `partial`. See §A0000000000 and §G #30.)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-08`: Closed/total Conway cert-state accumulation (fail-closed)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; delegation/pool state transitions); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B4 new rule (`status = "enforced"`); **strengthened by PHASE4-B5** (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B5`). Cross-refs `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-06`, `DC-LEDGER-07`, `T-DET-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, **`DC-LEDGER-09`** (now bidirectional — `DC-LEDGER-09` lists `DC-LEDGER-08` back), and **`DC-LEDGER-10`** (OQ5 — added bidirectionally; the cert-state this rule accumulates is now keyed on the discriminated `StakeCredential`, `DC-LEDGER-10` lists `DC-LEDGER-08` back). |
| **Requirement** | Conway cert-state accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition: certificates decode through the era-correct closed grammar (Conway via `decode_conway_certs` retaining all owner payloads, tags 0..18) selected by explicit era dispatch — never the Shelley 6-variant decoder on Conway bytes, never reduced into the 7-variant Shelley `Certificate`, never with payload fields dropped. Every certificate resolves to an owner-tagged disposition: it mutates B4-owned `CertState` (delegation/pool), or it is owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` and routed out-of-mutation-scope (observed, not swallowed), or it is a structured reject (`NotValidInEra` for removed tags 5/6, `Malformed` for bad CBOR, `UnsupportedUntilStateOwner` only for genuinely-ownerless cases). Composite certs (tags 10/12/13) carry both a B4-owned mutation and an owner-tagged governance effect; both are represented. No certificate is flattened to neutral, decode-dropped, or apply-swallowed; a decode or apply error propagates as a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition. Incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. (Wiring the owner-tagged `ConwayGovState` effects into applied governance state is PHASE4-B5, not B4. **As of PHASE4-B5 this disposition is strengthened: governance certs are no longer observed-and-dropped but applied to `ConwayGovState` — see `DC-LEDGER-09`.**) |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (owner-complete `ConwayCert` — every variant retains its owner payloads); `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`PoolRegistrationCert.owners`); `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_conway_certs` payload retention + `decode_drep`, total over tags 0..18); `crates/ade_codec/src/shelley/cert.rs` (shared `read_pool_registration_cert`) — PHASE4-B4-S1 decoder-completeness clause; `crates/ade_ledger/src/delegation.rs` (`apply_conway_cert` + the owner-tagged `ConwayCertAction` / `ConwayCertOutcome` apply model, total over the 18 tags) — PHASE4-B4-S2 apply-totality clause; `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`accumulate_tx_certs`, era-dispatched fail-closed — the Conway path runs the Conway decoder + apply model, the Shelley path the Shelley decoder; a decode or apply `Err` propagates and halts, never swallowed) — PHASE4-B4-S3/S4. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_decode_complete.rs::{each_tag_retains_owner_payloads, drep_grammar_total}` (decoder completeness — every tag retains its owner payloads, DRep grammar total); `crates/ade_ledger/src/delegation.rs::tests::{conway_cert_action_total, apply_outcome_agrees_with_action, removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid, drep_registration_is_owner_tagged_not_applied}` (apply model total + owner-tagged routing); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::tests::{era_dispatch_conway_accumulates_via_conway_path, era_dispatch_shelley_accumulates_via_shelley_path, conway_decode_error_is_fail_closed, conway_unknown_tag_is_fail_closed, conway_removed_tag_is_fail_closed, conway_apply_error_is_fail_closed, conway_governance_cert_routed_out_of_scope}` (era dispatch + fail-closed propagation + governance routing); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/cert_state_corpus.rs::{positive_synthetic_cert_state_accumulates, cert_state_replay_byte_identical, adversarial_no_false_accept}` (synthetic positive accumulation, byte-identical replay, adversarial no-false-accept — the B4 cert-state corpus, distinct from the same-named conservation-adversarial test). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` — extended in PHASE4-B4-S3/S4 to guard the cert-state fail-open swallow: it FAILs CI if the `"non-fatal during replay"` rationale string reappears anywhere under `crates/`, and if `accumulate_tx_certs` in `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` contains an `Err(_)` swallow arm. Gate PASSES at HEAD `ee35493` (verified during this refresh, exit 0). _(Enforcement gap, surfaced honestly — see §A0000: the real epoch-576 cert-state-vs-cardano-node oracle is **environment-blocked** (the epoch-576 UMap snapshot is absent post-extraction; see `corpus/cert_state/README.md`). Reclassified environment-blocked per tier doctrine — identical to the documented open obligation on `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-03`. Mechanical closure IS shipped — owner-complete decode + total owner-tagged apply + era-dispatched fail-closed accumulation + synthetic positive / replay / adversarial corpus; real-chain agreement remains the open obligation.)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-09`: Closed/total Conway governance-certificate accumulation (fail-closed)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL governance cert tags 9..18; `CONWAY` CERTS/GOVCERT/COMMITTEE transitions; CIP-1694); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B5 new rule (`status = "enforced"`). Cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-08`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-06`, `T-DET-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, and (OQ5) **`DC-LEDGER-10`** — all bidirectional at HEAD `a3ee2da` (the six target rules list `DC-LEDGER-09` back). OQ5 graduates `DC-LEDGER-09`'s prior OQ-5 `open_obligation` declared follow-up into the enforced `DC-LEDGER-10`: the `ConwayGovState` keys this rule accumulates are now the discriminated `StakeCredential`, not bare `Hash28`. |
| **Requirement** | Conway governance-certificate accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition into `ConwayGovState`: every governance-affecting Conway cert that B4 owner-tagged to `ConwayGovState` (vote-delegation tags 9/10/12/13 → `vote_delegations`; committee tags 14/15 → `committee_hot_keys`; DRep tags 16/17/18 → `drep_expiry`) resolves to exactly one explicit `ConwayGovState` mutation or a structured reject — never observed-and-dropped, never flattened, never with payload fields lost. B5 mutates only governance-owned fields; it does not touch B4-owned `CertState` and does not double-apply the delegation/pool half of composite certs (10/12/13). DRep expiry is computed only from an explicit gov-env (current epoch + `drepActivity`); a missing required env input is a structured fail-fast (`MissingDRepActivityParam`), never a defaulted expiry; expiry arithmetic is checked (`DRepActivityOverflow`). A cert that cannot be applied propagates a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition; incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. `ConwayGovState` becomes a deterministic function of (boundary-loaded base then replayed block-stream cert effects) rather than a frozen snapshot — a deliberate, oracle-confirmable fingerprint migration (`T-DET-01`). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs` (`apply_conway_gov_cert` — native gov dispatch over `ConwayCert`, total over the 18 tags, no `_ =>` wildcard) — PHASE4-B5-S2; `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`GovCertEnv` + `LedgerState::gov_cert_env()`, the sole fail-fast `GovCertEnv` constructor) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams.drep_activity`) + `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingDRepActivityParam`, `DRepActivityOverflow`) — PHASE4-B5-S1; `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`accumulate_tx_certs` / `process_block_certificates` thread `Option<ConwayGovState>`, apply the gov half, carry `gov_state` forward through `apply_block` — replaces the B4 observe-and-drop) — PHASE4-B5-S3; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (gov-state + `drep_activity` fingerprint surface). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/gov_cert.rs::tests::{gov_apply_total_over_18_tags, composite_gov_half_applied_once_certstate_untouched_by_b5, drep_expiry_uses_epoch_plus_activity, env_free_gov_certs_need_no_env, drep_register_missing_env_is_fail_fast, drep_expiry_overflow_is_fail_closed, gov_apply_is_deterministic}` (total gov dispatch, composite single-apply, DRep-expiry from env, env-free certs need no env, env fail-fast, overflow fail-closed, determinism); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs::tests::{gov_cert_env_present_ok, gov_cert_env_missing_drep_activity_is_fail_fast}` (env constructor present + fail-fast); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::tests::{gov_accumulation_applies_drep_registration_into_gov_state, gov_apply_error_halts_accumulation}` (block-path accumulation applies into gov state + halts on error); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/gov_state_corpus.rs::{positive_synthetic_gov_state_accumulates, gov_state_accumulation_replays_byte_identical, adversarial_drep_register_update_missing_env_rejected, adversarial_drep_expiry_overflow_rejected, adversarial_decode_layer_rejects_guard_gov_path, adversarial_double_resign_is_deterministic}` (synthetic positive accumulation, byte-identical replay, and the four adversarial no-false-accept / fail-fast / determinism corpus tests). All 17 confirmed to exist as functions at HEAD `651adc9`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh` — **new in PHASE4-B5**, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-09` in its header comment. It FAILs CI if (1) `apply_conway_gov_cert`'s match over `ConwayCert` gains a `_ =>` wildcard arm (adding a `ConwayCert` variant must break the build, never silently drop a governance effect); (2) the B4 observe-and-drop returns — the "routed out of B4 mutation scope" comment must not reappear and `accumulate_tx_certs` must call `apply_conway_gov_cert`; (3) the DRep-expiry env fail-fast is removed — `MissingDRepActivityParam` must exist and `gov_cert_env()` must be the only `GovCertEnv` constructor. Gate PASSES at HEAD `651adc9` (verified during this refresh, exit 0). Plus `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (bidirectional `cross_ref` enforcement — now PASSES with `DC-LEDGER-09`/`DC-LEDGER-08` bidirectional). _(Enforcement gap, surfaced honestly — see §A00000 and §G #19: the real epoch-576 governance-state (VState)-vs-cardano-node oracle is **environment-blocked** (the epoch-576 UMap/ledger snapshot is absent post-extraction; see `corpus/gov_state/README.md`, `corpus/cert_state/README.md`, `corpus/validity/conway_epoch576/README.md`). Reclassified environment-blocked per tier doctrine — identical to the documented open obligations on `DC-LEDGER-08` / `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-03`. Mechanical closure IS shipped — native total gov dispatch + env fail-fast + checked DRep-expiry arithmetic + block-path accumulation + synthetic positive/replay/adversarial corpus; real-chain agreement remains the open obligation. **Two declared separable follow-ups (NOT part of this closure):** OQ-3 — the GOVCERT committee-membership tx-validity gate (§G #20); OQ-5 — `ConwayGovState` keys gov state on bare `Hash28` and the codec collapses the key/script credential discriminant (`ade_codec` `decode_stake_credential` drops the type tag), so a key-hash and script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are indistinguishable in `vote_delegations`/`committee_hot_keys`/`drep_expiry`; cardano-node keys on the full discriminated `Credential`. Pre-existing decoder behaviour newly promoted to authority by B5, tracked per the per-cluster security review (§G #21).)_ |

### `DC-LEDGER-10`: Credential key/script discriminant fidelity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (`Credential = key|script` across UTXOW/DELEG/GOVCERT; CIP-1694); IDD illegal-states-unrepresentable + determinism doctrine. OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY new rule (`status = "enforced"`); **strengthened by COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY, AGAIN by DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY, AGAIN by ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY** (`strengthened_in = ["COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY", "DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY", "ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY", "ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK"]` — the committee-credential, DRep-voter, dormant committee-enactment-effect, and now the **live committee-enactment write-back** halves of the same discriminant-fidelity work; still one rule, still `enforced`, no new rule added by any strengthening). Origin: the PHASE4-B5 per-cluster security review (WARN/MEDIUM) + `DC-LEDGER-09`'s `open_obligation` (the prior §G #21 OQ-5 declared follow-up — now graduated into this enforced rule). Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-ENC-03`, `DC-LEDGER-08`, `DC-LEDGER-09`, `DC-TXV-05`, **and `DC-LEDGER-11` (PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE, added bidirectionally — the new typed Conway `proposal_procedures` decode preserves the `UpdateCommittee` discriminant this rule defines; `DC-LEDGER-11` lists `DC-LEDGER-10` back)** — all bidirectional (the six target rules list `DC-LEDGER-10` back). `DC-LEDGER-10` *strengthens* `T-DET-01` / `T-ENC-03` and *relates* `DC-LEDGER-08` / `DC-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05`. |
| **Requirement** | Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential is a closed sum over `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` of a 28-byte hash, never a tag-erased `Hash28`. Both era certificate decoders preserve the key/script discriminant (an unknown tag is a deterministic reject); the credential type makes a discriminant-less credential unrepresentable on the BLUE authority path (no `Hash28`→credential coercion); `CertState` (registrations/delegations/rewards) and `ConwayGovState` (vote_delegations/committee_hot_keys/drep_expiry) key on the discriminated credential, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are distinct authoritative-state keys (matching cardano-node's `Credential`-keyed UMap/VState); and the canonical fingerprint serializes the discriminant so two states differing only in a credential's key/script tag fingerprint differently. The discriminated representation is a deliberate cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration (`T-DET-01`). Default scope is Shelley+; Byron is included only if proven to have an affected credential surface. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_types/src/shelley/cert.rs` (`StakeCredential` closed `enum {KeyHash(Hash28), ScriptHash(Hash28)}` + `hash()` accessor — replaces the tuple-struct `StakeCredential(Hash28)`) — OQ5-S1; ### `DC-LEDGER-11`: Conway proposal_procedures is a closed typed grammar (no opaque bytes)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | CIP-1694 (`proposal_procedure = [coin, reward_account, gov_action, anchor]`); Project constitution §3 (closed semantic surfaces, `T-CORE-01`); `DC-LEDGER-10` (downstream credential discriminant must not be re-collapsed). PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE new rule (`status = "enforced"`, `introduced_in = "PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE"`, `strengthened_in = []`). Cross-ref `["DC-LEDGER-10"]` — bidirectional (`DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` lists `DC-LEDGER-11` back). The pairing is structural: PP-S1 reuses the existing closed `GovAction` enum (the `UpdateCommittee` arm carries the structured `{removed, added, threshold}` with `StakeCredential` cold members from ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK), so the new typed `proposal_procedures` decode cannot re-collapse the committee credential discriminant `DC-LEDGER-10` defends. |
| **Requirement** | `proposal_procedures` MUST NOT remain an opaque byte field in the authoritative Conway tx-body shape. `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>`, decoded through a single closed entry point (`decode_proposal_procedures`) that rejects unknown `gov_action` tags, structural failures, empty sets, and trailing garbage deterministically; the typed form re-encodes byte-identically (`PreservedCbor`) for every well-formed Conway tx body. The decoder reuses the existing closed `GovAction` enum (preserving `DC-LEDGER-10` `UpdateCommittee` discriminant) and the existing opaque `Anchor` struct. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` — PP-S1: `decode_proposal_procedures` (the single sanctioned entry point: array-of-procedures with rejected empty set + rejected trailing bytes), `decode_proposal_procedure` (the per-procedure 4-tuple `[deposit, return_addr, gov_action, anchor]`), `decode_gov_action` (closed dispatch over every CIP-1694 tag — `ParameterChange`, `HardForkInitiation`, `TreasuryWithdrawals`, `NoConfidence`, `UpdateCommittee`, `NewConstitution`, `InfoAction` — unknown tag rejects deterministically), `encode_proposal_procedures` (byte-identical round-trip). `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` — PP-S1: `ProposalProcedure` closed struct `{ deposit: Coin, return_addr: RewardAccount-as-bytes, gov_action: GovAction, anchor: Anchor }`. `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/tx.rs` — PP-S1: the typed key 20 path on `ConwayTxBody` calls `decode_proposal_procedures` / `encode_proposal_procedures` (no `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through anywhere on key 20). `crates/ade_testkit/src/governance/proposal_procedures_replay.rs` — PP-S2: the canonical synthetic corpus (covers every `GovAction` variant + a deliberate `UpdateCommittee` `KeyHash`/`ScriptHash` discriminant case + multi-procedure containers) plus the replay harness driving the closed decoder + body-codec round-trips byte-identically. |
| **Tests** | PP-S1 inline in `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` (14 unit tests): `roundtrip_info_action_proposal`, `roundtrip_hard_fork_initiation`, `roundtrip_no_confidence`, `roundtrip_treasury_withdrawals`, `roundtrip_parameter_change`, `roundtrip_new_constitution`, `roundtrip_update_committee`, `roundtrip_multi_procedure` (every `GovAction` variant + multi-procedure containers re-encode byte-identically), `rejects_unknown_gov_action_tag`, `rejects_empty_proposal_procedures_set`, `rejects_trailing_garbage`, `rejects_truncated_proposal_procedure`, `rejects_invalid_stake_credential_in_update_committee` (adversarial guarantees: unknown tag / empty set / trailing bytes / truncated payload / malformed nested credential all reject deterministically), `update_committee_keeps_stake_credential_discriminant` (the `DC-LEDGER-10` `UpdateCommittee` discriminant survives the new decode). PP-S1 integration in `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_tx_body_proposal_procedures.rs` (3 tests): `body_with_proposal_procedures_round_trips_through_typed_field` (the typed key-20 path round-trips on a full `ConwayTxBody`), `body_none_skips_proposal_procedures_key_20` (`None` does not emit key 20 at all — the negative shape), `body_and_sub_decoder_agree_on_proposal_procedures` (the body-level decode and the sub-decoder agree byte-for-byte on the same input). PP-S2 corpus tests in `crates/ade_testkit/tests/proposal_procedures_corpus_replay.rs` (4 tests): `canonical_corpus_decodes_to_expected_shape` (every canonical-corpus entry decodes into the expected typed shape), `canonical_corpus_round_trips_byte_identical` (encode-after-decode is byte-identical on every entry), `canonical_corpus_covers_all_gov_action_variants` (the corpus exercises every `GovAction` variant — the coverage gate the harness was built around), `canonical_corpus_includes_update_committee_discriminant_case` (the corpus contains the `UpdateCommittee` `KeyHash` + `ScriptHash` cold-member case that pins the `DC-LEDGER-10` pairing). All **21** confirmed to exist as functions in the codebase at HEAD `928c2be` (grep-verified during this refresh). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` — **new in PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE PP-S1**, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-11` in its header comment. Five mechanical guards: (1) `ade_types::conway::governance` defines the closed `ProposalProcedure` struct with all four fields (`pub deposit`, `pub return_addr`, `pub gov_action`, `pub anchor`); (2) `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` is declared `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` — NOT `Option<Vec<u8>>` (the prior opaque form); (3) `ade_codec::conway::governance` exists and exports both `decode_proposal_procedures` and `encode_proposal_procedures`; (4) the Conway tx-body codec at key 20 calls the typed decoder/encoder and does NOT use the prior `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through for `proposal_procedures`; (5) no `ProposalProcedure {` struct-literal construction outside the sanctioned synthesis sites (`ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs`, `ade_testkit/`, `crates/*/tests/`, and `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` blocks — production callers MUST go through `decode_proposal_procedures`). Gate is expected to PASS at HEAD `928c2be` (PP-S1 + PP-S2 land the surface this gate defends). Plus `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (bidirectional `cross_ref` enforcement — `DC-LEDGER-11.cross_ref = ["DC-LEDGER-10"]` is bidirectional with `DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` listing `DC-LEDGER-11` back; expected PASS at 176 entries). _(Open obligations recorded in `DC-LEDGER-11.open_obligation`, NOT enforcement gaps: OQ-1 — `voting_procedures` (tx body key 19) closure is the natural sibling cluster, same opaque-bytes shape, deliberately deferred and explicitly NOT covered by this rule. OQ-2 / OQ-3 — `ParameterChange.update` and `NewConstitution.raw` nested opacities are likewise deferred; they are future `strengthened_in` candidates if/when those sub-grammars are closed. OQ-4 — typed `RewardAccount` for `proposal_procedure.return_addr` is a separate fidelity decision. See §A000000000000 and §G #32.)_ |

### `DC-MEM-01`: Mempool rules subset of block/ledger rules

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-DET-01`, `T-CORE-01`. Flipped `declared -> enforced` by PHASE4-B2. **Strengthened AGAIN by PHASE4-N-E** (`strengthened_in = ["PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-N-E"]`): admission is now reached only through the closed wire-level `mempool_ingress(IngressEvent)` chokepoint; the source variant (`N2N` / `N2C`) is evidence/policy/replay metadata and MUST NOT change the validity verdict. `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-03", "DC-MEM-04"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Mempool acceptance rules must not contradict block/ledger acceptance rules — a tx admitted to the mempool is exactly a tx that `tx_validity` deems `Valid` against the accumulating view; admission never accepts what block/ledger validity would reject. PHASE4-N-E adds: admission is identical when reached through `mempool_ingress(IngressEvent { source, tx_bytes })` versus direct `admit(state, tx_bytes)` — the bridge is a thin source-erasing relabel that preserves verdicts byte-for-byte. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/admit.rs` (admission delegates to `tx_validity` against the accumulating `MempoolState`; closed `AdmitOutcome`); plus PHASE4-N-E — `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` (`IngressEvent` / `IngressSource` closed types + the `mempool_ingress` single sanctioned production path into `admit`); `crates/ade_testkit/src/mempool/ingress_replay.rs` (GREEN harness `replay_ingress_trace`, `wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress` — exercises the bridge over the B-track corpus and asserts byte-identical verdicts vs direct admit). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_admission.rs::{valid_tx_admitted_and_accumulates, invalid_tx_rejected_no_false_accept, admission_equals_tx_validity_verdict, dependent_tx_admitted_against_accumulating_state}`; plus PHASE4-N-E `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_replay.rs::{ingress_admit_equals_direct_admit_on_b_track_corpus, b_track_adversarial_rejections_preserved_through_ingress, dependent_pair_through_ingress_admits_b_after_a}` (the bridge produces the same admit verdicts and the same accumulating state as direct admit on the entire B-track positive + adversarial corpus, including the load-bearing dependent-pair case where tx B depends on tx A and only the A→B order admits both). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (extended in B2 to scan `ade_ledger/src/mempool/` — `AdmitOutcome` must stay a closed structured value). Augmented in spirit by `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-E — forbids any production `admit` caller outside `mempool_ingress`, so the bridge is the only path into the BLUE admission verdict; the explicit anchor for that gate is `DC-MEM-03` but it structurally protects `DC-MEM-01`'s mempool-rules-equal-block-rules guarantee against future sideways-into-`admit` regressions). |

### `DC-MEM-02`: Deterministic overload shedding

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; refines `T-DET-01`, `T-CORE-02`. Flipped `declared -> enforced` by PHASE4-B2. |
| **Requirement** | Overload shedding follows a deterministic ordering policy, not timing-dependent collapse — the policy may decide *which* txs are kept under pressure but may never change a tx's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict (Tier-5 policy independence). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/policy.rs` (closed `OrderPolicy`; deterministic ordering independent of the validity verdict). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_admission.rs::{policy_does_not_change_validity, determinism}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (`OrderPolicy` must stay a closed structured value). |

### `DC-MEM-03`: Closed wire-level mempool ingress (source is metadata)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3, `T-CORE-01` (closed semantic surfaces), `DC-MEM-01`. Introduced by PHASE4-N-E (S1, commit `32c1ee6`). `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-01"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Tx ingress reduces to a closed `IngressEvent` before BLUE mempool admission; the source variant is evidence/policy/replay metadata only and MUST NOT change the validity verdict. `IngressSource` is the closed two-variant sum `{N2N, N2C}` (no `#[non_exhaustive]`, no open tail). `mempool_ingress` is the only sanctioned production path into `admit` — every other production caller is a closure violation. `MempoolState.accumulating` is constructed or replaced only inside `admit.rs`. The `mempool_ingress` body MUST NOT branch on `event.source` — that field is metadata. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` — `IngressEvent` (record carrying `source: IngressSource` + `tx_bytes: Vec<u8>`), `IngressSource` (closed `{N2N, N2C}`), `mempool_ingress(state, event) -> (MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` (the single BLUE bridge — pure relabel onto `admit` with the source discarded for verdict purposes). |
| **Tests** | Inline in `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs`: `ingress_preserves_tx_bytes_verbatim` (the `tx_bytes` field is forwarded byte-for-byte into `admit`), `ingress_source_is_closed_two_variants` (the enum has exactly two variants and is closed — structural assertion). Integration in `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_ingress.rs`: `ingress_admits_valid_tx_via_n2n`, `ingress_admits_valid_tx_via_n2c` (valid B-track tx admits through both source flavors), `ingress_rejects_invalid_tx_no_false_accept` (an invalid tx rejects through the bridge with the same `AdmitOutcome::Reject{...}` shape as direct admit — no false accept), `ingress_source_does_not_change_verdict_valid`, `ingress_source_does_not_change_verdict_adversarial` (the same `(state, tx_bytes)` produces byte-identical `(MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` under `N2N` vs `N2C` on both the positive and the adversarial corpora), `ingress_equals_direct_admit_on_synthetic_corpus` (on the synthetic corpus, the bridge's output equals direct `admit` element-wise). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_closure.sh` (PHASE4-N-E S1, anchored on `DC-MEM-03` in the script header). Five checks: (1) `ingress.rs` exists and defines `IngressSource` + `IngressEvent` + `mempool_ingress`; (2) `IngressSource` is a closed 2-variant enum (`N2N`, `N2C`), no `#[non_exhaustive]`; (3) `MempoolState.accumulating` is constructed/replaced only inside `admit.rs` (the only sanctioned production write site is the `accumulating: applied` field set in `admit()`); (4) `admit()` is called only from sanctioned production sites — `admit.rs` itself (definition + `#[cfg(test)]`) and `ingress.rs` (the bridge); any other `src/` caller is a closure violation, with `tests/` and `benches/` directories exempt; (5) `mempool_ingress`'s body does not branch on `event.source` — the source field is metadata only. |

### `DC-MEM-04`: Mempool ingress-trace replay is byte-identical

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3, `T-DET-01`, `DC-MEM-01`. Introduced by PHASE4-N-E (S2..S5, commits `2d0c918` → `509d714` → `ca3f23a` → `43fcc31`). `cross_ref = ["DC-MEM-01"]` (bidirectional). |
| **Requirement** | Replaying the same ordered ingress trace against the same base ledger state produces a byte-identical sequence of `(MempoolState, AdmitOutcome)` pairs. The replay is strictly single-step per OQ-6 (a fold over `mempool_ingress`, not a partition / batch). Multi-peer interleavings canonicalize to a deterministic round-robin order by sorted peer ID (S3/S4), so two interleavings of the same per-peer queues replay byte-identically. The GREEN harness goes through `mempool_ingress` (the BLUE bridge), never through `admit` directly — the replay is genuinely a fold over the BLUE chokepoint. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/mempool/ingress_replay.rs` (GREEN harness — `wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress`, `replay_ingress_trace`, `BTrackCase`, `ExpectedOutcome`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` (the BLUE bridge the fold drives); `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/canonicalize.rs` (deterministic canonical-order canonicalizer that round-robins per-peer `PeerSubmissionQueue`s by sorted `PeerId`, preserving tx bytes verbatim and propagating the source from the queue — S3/S4). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_replay.rs::{ingress_admit_equals_direct_admit_on_b_track_corpus, b_track_adversarial_rejections_preserved_through_ingress, ingress_trace_replay_byte_identical, dependent_pair_through_ingress_admits_b_after_a, ingress_trace_source_invariant_n2n_vs_n2c}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/canonicalize.rs` inline: `multi_peer_round_robin_by_sorted_peer_id` (multi-peer interleaving is canonicalized to a deterministic round-robin order by sorted peer ID — S4), `unsorted_input_canonicalizes_identically_to_sorted_input` (unsorted peer input canonicalizes to the same output as sorted input — S4); `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_canonicalize.rs::two_interleavings_replay_byte_identical` (two distinct interleavings of the same per-peer queues replay byte-identically through the canonical order — S5). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_mempool_ingress_replay.sh` (PHASE4-N-E S2, anchored on `DC-MEM-04` in the script header). Four checks: (1) the GREEN harness module exists and exports the four items (`wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress`, `replay_ingress_trace`, `BTrackCase` + `ExpectedOutcome`); (2) the harness's `replay_ingress_trace` body uses `mempool_ingress` — NOT direct `admit` calls — so the replay is genuinely a fold over the BLUE chokepoint; (3) the four load-bearing test names referenced by the registry's `DC-MEM-04.tests` array exist in the integration test file; (4) the harness contains no batching / out-of-order helpers — the replay is strictly single-step per OQ-6 (`fold`, not `partition`). |

### `DC-CORE-01`: BLUE crates are sync-only (no async); BLUE consensus ⇎ ChainDb

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2, `T-CORE-02`; PHASE4-N-A scope decisions §Decision 2 (`docs/active/PHASE4-N-A_scope_decisions.md`); strengthened by PHASE4-N-B over `ade_core::consensus` + `ade_runtime::consensus`. |
| **Requirement** | BLUE authoritative crates are sync-only: no `async fn`, `.await`, `tokio::`, `async_std::`, `Future`, `futures::`, task spawning, async channels, or timers. Async runtime concerns are confined to RED transport/runtime code. PHASE4-N-B narrows further: BLUE consensus (`ade_core::consensus`) may not reference `ChainDb`/`chain_db` — those belong to RED `ade_runtime::chaindb`. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/chain_selector.rs` (GREEN orchestrator that bridges BLUE consensus transitions to RED N-A network inputs; never receives sockets or tokio types); `crates/ade_core_interop/src/lib.rs` + `crates/ade_core_interop/src/bin/live_consensus_session.rs` (RED live-peer driver crate; depends on ade_core only via typed Orchestrator surface). |
| **Tests** | `consensus::chain_selector::tests::{header_arrival_updates_state_and_selector, rollback_walks_back_via_recent_snapshots, rollback_to_block_older_than_snapshots_rejected, epoch_boundary_emits_no_event}`; `crates/ade_core_interop/tests/live_consensus_session.rs::cardano_node_session_sustained_window` (`#[ignore]` by default). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_no_async_in_blue.sh` — bans `async fn`/`.await`/`tokio::`/`async_std::`/`Future`/`futures::`/spawn/timers anywhere in BLUE; scans all 6 BLUE crates plus the 9 `ade_network` submodule paths and `crates/ade_core/`. `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh` (PHASE4-N-B) — bans `ChainDb`/`chain_db` tokens anywhere under `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/`. Together they discharge the BLUE/RED partition for consensus. |

### `DC-PROTO-06`: BLUE protocol transitions are pure functions of explicit version

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §2; PHASE4-N-A invariants §7 decision 1 (`docs/active/PHASE4-N-A_invariants.md`). |
| **Requirement** | BLUE mini-protocol transitions are pure functions of (canonical prior state, canonical input message, selected protocol version, deterministic configuration); no ambient session-glue state may alter authoritative behavior. Selected version is an explicit input, never read from RED context. |
| **Code** | Per-protocol pure transition modules under `crates/ade_network/src/{chain_sync,block_fetch,tx_submission,keep_alive,peer_sharing}/{state,agency,signal,event,transition}.rs` plus the four N2C state machines under `crates/ade_network/src/n2c/{local_chain_sync,local_tx_submission,local_state_query,local_tx_monitor}/{state,agency,event,transition}.rs`. All transition signatures take selected protocol version as an explicit typed parameter. |
| **Tests** | Same large per-protocol transition battery as `DC-PROTO-01` — the `version_gating_rejects_out_of_version_message` test on every state machine is the explicit DC-PROTO-06 evidence anchor, plus the per-protocol `wrong_agency_returns_error` tests and the event-trace corpora. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_ce_n_a_5_proof.sh` (CE-N-A-5 condition 2 — version-gating rejection across all 11 protocols). |

| **Requirement** | Praos chain selection ordering: block number first, then Praos `TiebreakerView` (slot, issuer, op-cert issue number, VRF output). Density-based ordering is reserved for Genesis/catch-up and must not be used for caught-up Praos fork-choice. |

### `DC-CONS-04`: Praos chain-dep state authority (consensus-owned, not ledger)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus `PraosChainDepState`; cross-refs `DC-CONSENSUS-02`, `DC-CONS-10`. |
