| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/praos_state.rs` (`PraosChainDepState` + op-cert counter `BTreeMap`); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/events.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/errors.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/encoding.rs` (canonical state encoding); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/nonce.rs` (`apply_nonce_input` + epoch-boundary rotation); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/op_cert.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/header_validate.rs`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/header_summary.rs`. |
| **Tests** | `consensus::praos_state::tests::{op_cert_upsert_rejects_regression, op_cert_upsert_rejects_equal_counter, op_cert_upsert_accepts_strictly_increasing, genesis_state_is_well_formed, nonce_zero_constant_is_zero_bytes}`; `consensus::encoding::tests::op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic`; canonical-roundtrip battery `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_state_canonical_roundtrip.rs::{layout_is_stable, roundtrip_empty_state, roundtrip_genesis_state, roundtrip_populated_state, roundtrip_chain_event_all_variants, roundtrip_chain_selection_reject_all_variants, decode_rejects_unknown_discriminant, decode_rejects_short_array, op_cert_counter_map_iteration_is_deterministic}`; nonce evolution `consensus::nonce::tests::*` (11 unit tests) + `crates/ade_core/tests/nonce_evolution_corpus.rs::{within_epoch_evolving_nonce_matches_corpus, epoch_boundary_freezes_and_rotates_correctly, nonce_evolution_replay_is_deterministic}`; op-cert `consensus::op_cert::tests::*` (8 unit tests) + `crates/ade_core/tests/op_cert_counter_corpus.rs::{normal_progression_records_highest_counter_per_window, regression_after_progression_rejected_with_typed_error, op_cert_replay_is_deterministic}`; header-validate `consensus::header_validate::tests::{pipeline_short_circuits_on_first_failure, nonce_contribution_uses_nonce_role_vrf_output_not_leader_role}` + `crates/ade_core/tests/header_validate_compose.rs::{valid_header_accepted_advances_state, header_with_slot_regression_rejected, header_with_block_no_regression_rejected, header_with_op_cert_regression_rejected, header_with_invalid_vrf_proof_rejected, header_beyond_forecast_horizon_rejected, validate_replay_is_deterministic}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (no `#[non_exhaustive]`, no `Other`/`Unknown` open-tail variants, no owned `String` or `Box<dyn>` in `errors.rs`/`encoding.rs`/`events.rs`). |

### `DC-CONS-05`: Rollback bounded by k blocks

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; ouroboros-consensus consensus report; cross-refs `DC-CONS-06`, `CN-CONS-01`. |
| **Requirement** | Authoritative rollback must never exceed the security parameter k measured in blocks (mainnet k = 2160). Rollback requests deeper than k return `ExceededRollback`. Forecast/stability windows may be slot-based but must accommodate at least k+1 blocks. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/rollback.rs::apply_rollback`; `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/events.rs` (`ChainEvent::RollBack`, `ChainSelectionReject::ExceededRollback` / `ForkBeforeImmutableTip`). |
| **Tests** | Unit-level `consensus::rollback::tests::{rollback_preserves_immutable_tip, rollback_preserves_security_param, rollback_with_zero_depth_is_noop, rollback_to_equal_block_no_as_immutable_succeeds, rollback_to_one_below_immutable_rejected}`; corpus tests `crates/ade_core/tests/rollback_corpus.rs::{rollback_within_k_succeeds, rollback_exceeding_k_rejected_with_typed_reason, rollback_before_immutable_tip_rejected, rollback_event_bytes_are_stable, rollback_is_deterministic, rollback_equivalent_to_truncated_replay}` (CE-N-B-2). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`, `ci/ci_check_no_chaindb_in_consensus_blue.sh`. |

### `DC-CONS-06`: Rollback = truncated replay; immutable tip final

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §3; `T-DET-01`; cross-refs `DC-CONS-05`, `T-DET-01`. |
| **Requirement** | `rollback(state, depth)` produces state byte-identical to truncated replay from the nearest checkpoint. Rollback that would cross the immutable tip (≥ k deep) returns `ForkBeforeImmutableTip` and never alters state. |

### `DC-VAL-01`: Validity verdict is a pure function of canonical inputs

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; Ouroboros Praos spec; IDD determinism doctrine (cross-refs `DC-CORE-01`, `T-DET-01`, `DC-CONSENSUS-01`). |
| **Requirement** | A block's validity verdict is a pure function of `(LedgerState, PraosChainDepState, EraSchedule, LedgerView, block_cbor)`. No wall-clock, arrival order, `HashMap`/`HashSet` iteration, float, or ambient state may influence it. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_input_extract.rs` (canonical nonce/field projection), `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_view.rs` (pure ledger-side `LedgerView` impl), `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/ledger_view.rs` (`LedgerView` trait — extractive forecast surface). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/consensus_input_extract.rs::tests::{extract_nonces_field_order, extract_nonces_requires_exactly_five, extract_nonces_is_deterministic}`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/consensus_view.rs::{view_returns_corpus_pool_stake_and_vrf_keyhash, view_unknown_pool_returns_none, view_unknown_epoch_returns_none, view_is_pure}`; corpus self-consistency `corpus_loads_and_is_self_consistent`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally over the BLUE tree by `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` (no `HashMap`/`HashSet`/float/wall-clock in BLUE) and, for the consensus inputs, `ci/ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`. No `ci/ci_check_block_validity.sh` exists — see §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-02`: Valid iff header AND body authority accept

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; Ouroboros Praos spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `CN-CONS-04`, `DC-CONS-04`). |
| **Requirement** | A block is `Valid` iff both the consensus header authority (`validate_and_apply_header`) and the ledger body authority (`apply_block_with_verdicts`) accept it. No path may produce a `Valid` verdict while skipping either authority. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed verdict/error taxonomy substrate); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` + `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/header_input.rs` (header ∧ body composition — header authority decided, then body authority applied). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_compose.rs::{valid_block_evolves_both_states, header_before_body_fail_fast}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally by `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` keeping the verdict/error taxonomy closed. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-03`: Header-before-body fail-fast ordering

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Ouroboros Praos spec; IDD fail-fast doctrine (cross-refs `DC-VAL-02`). |
| **Requirement** | The header is validated before the body; body validation never runs on a header-invalid block. The first failing authority determines the reason. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (header authority decided before body; body authority unreachable on header failure). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_compose.rs::header_before_body_fail_fast`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-04`: Verdict agrees with reference (positive + adversarial)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | cardano-node reference behavior; Cardano ledger spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `CN-LEDGER-02`). |
| **Requirement** | Ade's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict for a block equals the reference cardano-node verdict, including the reason class where the reference exposes it — established over both a positive corpus (real valid blocks) and a mandatory adversarial corpus (blocks the reference rejects). |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed `Valid`/`Invalid` + reject-class comparison surface); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/replay.rs` (GREEN positive-corpus replay over all 14 Conway-576 blocks); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (GREEN deterministic mutators M1–M6 deriving adversarial blocks from the real corpus). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_positive_corpus.rs::{corpus_block_count_is_14, all_corpus_blocks_valid, verdict_stream_replays_identically}`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class, adversarial_replays_identically}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via positive + adversarial corpus test surface. The CE-B1-4 no-false-accept property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) and the 14/14 positive-corpus property (`all_corpus_blocks_valid`) have no CI gate. See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-05`: Total state evolution (invalid → unchanged)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD explicit-total-transition doctrine; Cardano ledger spec (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`). |
| **Requirement** | A `Valid` block yields evolved `(LedgerState', PraosChainDepState')`; an `Invalid` block yields the unchanged input states plus a structured reason. No partial or in-place mutation occurs on the invalid path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` (closed verdict taxonomy: `Valid` carries evolved-state stats, `Invalid` carries a structured reason); `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs` (`Valid` returns evolved `(ledger', chain_dep')`; `Invalid` returns input clones). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_compose.rs::{invalid_block_leaves_state_unchanged, valid_block_evolves_both_states}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `enforced` via test surface only. Discharged structurally by `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (closed verdict taxonomy). See §A0 / §G.)_ |

### `DC-VAL-06`: Fail-closed field checks (no silent skip)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (mandatory witness/field checks); IDD fail-fast doctrine (cross-refs `DC-LEDGER-02`, `T-ENC-01`, `DC-CRYPTO-01`, `DC-TXV-06`). Strengthened by PHASE4-B1 (block fail-closed field checks), PHASE4-B2 (tx witness/input fail-closed checks), PHASE4-B3 (cert/withdrawal conservation early-out removed), PHASE4-B3F (decoder strictness), and PHASE4-B4 (cert-state silent-skip removal). |
| **Requirement** | Every crypto-input, field-size, and structural check on the authority path rejects (produces `Invalid`) on wrong size or shape and never silently skips. The pattern `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` is forbidden in BLUE validation; size checks go through a helper that returns an error. No defined-but-unwired check and no tautological (value-compared-to-itself) guard may stand in for a real check. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs` (`FieldKind`/`FieldError` closed fail-closed field taxonomy); `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs` (`expect_size` fail-closed header crypto-field guard); `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (M1 truncated VRF proof, M3 flipped KES sig, M4 slot-beyond-horizon mutators); plus PHASE4-B2 tx-path fail-closed checks — `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs` (wrong-size vkey/sig -> `MalformedWitnessField` via `from_bytes`, never skipped) and `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs` (unresolvable input / collateral input is fail-fast, never a silent skip); plus PHASE4-B3 — `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` no longer carries the cert/withdrawal early-out (the B2 `if certs.is_some() || withdrawals.is_some() { skip }` fail-open is **removed**), so a cert/withdrawal-bearing imbalanced tx is now rejected on value grounds rather than silently skipped; the §9.1 reject-precedence ordering is deterministic; plus PHASE4-B3F — `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs::decode_conway_certs` now rejects trailing bytes after the cert array (`CodecError::TrailingBytes`) and bounds preallocation against a hostile array count, closing two fail-open decoder paths; plus PHASE4-B4 — `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs::accumulate_tx_certs` no longer swallows a cert-state decode/apply `Err` (the prior "non-fatal during replay" silent-skip is **removed**), so a Conway cert that fails to decode or apply now propagates a structured `LedgerError` and halts the block transition rather than being silently skipped (see `DC-LEDGER-08`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs::tests::expect_size_rejects_wrong_length`; `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_header_validate.rs::praos_malformed_kes_sig_rejected`; `crates/ade_ledger/tests/block_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class}`; plus PHASE4-B2 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_witness_closure.rs::{wrong_size_signature_rejected, wrong_size_vkey_rejected, unresolvable_input_is_fail_fast, unresolvable_collateral_input_is_fail_fast}`; plus PHASE4-B3 `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_full.rs::{conway_conservation_full, conservation_early_out_removed, reject_reason_precedence_is_deterministic, state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects}` and the adversarial suite `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_adversarial.rs::{adversarial_imbalanced_via_deposit, adversarial_imbalanced_via_withdrawal, adversarial_unknown_cert_tag_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid, adversarial_truncated_withdrawals_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects, adversarial_no_false_accept, adversarial_verdicts_replay_byte_identical}`; plus PHASE4-B3F decoder-strictness `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{trailing_bytes_after_cert_array_rejected, huge_array_count_rejects_without_overallocating}` (the cert-array decoder rejects trailing bytes and bounds preallocation, never silently truncating or over-allocating on a hostile count). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (keeps the block-validity AND tx-validity reject/field/signer taxonomies closed over `ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` and `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`). `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1", "PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-B3", "PHASE4-B3F", "PHASE4-B4"]`. PHASE4-B4 also wires `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` as a complementary fail-open guard (it FAILs if the cert-state `"non-fatal during replay"` swallow rationale or an `Err(_)` swallow arm in `accumulate_tx_certs` reappears — see `DC-LEDGER-08`). PHASE4-B5 adds `DC-LEDGER-09` to `DC-VAL-06`'s `cross_ref` (bidirectional): governance-cert accumulation extends the fail-closed/no-silent-skip discipline to the `ConwayGovState` mutation surface, defended by the new `ci/ci_check_gov_cert_accumulation_closed.sh`. The general fail-open-pattern ban (`if X.len()==K { } else { skip }`) is still **not** mechanically text-scanned — proven only by the adversarial corpora plus the B3 `conservation_early_out_removed` regression test. See §G — strong candidate for a new `ci/ci_check_no_fail_open_len_guard.sh`. |

---

### `DC-TXV-01`: Pure tx_validity

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec; IDD determinism doctrine (cross-refs `T-DET-01`). PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | `tx_validity` is a pure function of `(LedgerState, tx_cbor)`. No wall-clock, arrival order, `HashMap`/`HashSet` iteration, float, or ambient state may influence a transaction's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/transition.rs` (`tx_validity`: pure composition over `(&LedgerState, &[u8])`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (`tx_phase_one` + `decode_tx`, no I/O / clock / rand). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::tx_validity_is_deterministic`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (closed verdict taxonomy over `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`); discharged structurally over the BLUE tree by `ci/ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` (no `HashMap`/`HashSet`/float/wall-clock in BLUE). |

### `DC-TXV-02`: Phase-1 AND phase-2

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (UTXOW/UTXO/PPUP, Plutus phase-2). PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | A transaction is `Valid` iff both phase-1 (structural + UTxO rules + witnesses) and phase-2 (Plutus, when scripts are present) accept it. No path may produce a `Valid` verdict while skipping either phase. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/transition.rs` (`tx_validity`: fail-fast — phase-1 decided first; phase-2 dispatch via `plutus_eval::try_evaluate_tx` never runs when phase-1 fails or when no Plutus scripts are present); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (`tx_phase_one` composes the B2-S1 witness closure + `validate_conway_state_backed`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::{valid_tx_is_valid_and_applies, phase1_failure_short_circuits_phase2}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. |

### `DC-TXV-03`: Verdict agreement (positive + adversarial)

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | cardano-node reference behavior; Cardano ledger spec. PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | Ade's `Valid`/`Invalid` verdict for a transaction equals the reference cardano-node verdict, including the reason class where the reference exposes it — established over a positive corpus (real on-chain txs) and a mandatory adversarial corpus (txs the reference rejects). A false-accept is release-blocking. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/` (GREEN harness: extracts every on-wire Conway tx from the committed Conway-576 corpus blocks and drives the BLUE `tx_validity` over each — partial scope at `track_utxo=false`: structural + witness closure; UTxO-dependent checks deferred); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/phase1.rs` (`tx_phase_one` gates the UTxO-dependent state-backed checks behind `track_utxo`, mirroring the block path's `verify_conway_witness_closure` + `run_phase_one_composers` split — the witness closure runs unconditionally); `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/adversarial.rs` (B2 adversarial half); plus PHASE4-B3 — the cert/withdrawal-bearing positive corpora (real + synthetic) and the adversarial conservation corpus exercise the now-full coin-conservation path. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_positive_corpus.rs::{corpus_tx_count_nonzero, all_corpus_txs_valid}` (real Conway txs all `Valid`); `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_adversarial_corpus.rs::{no_mutation_is_ever_valid, each_mutation_maps_to_expected_class, adversarial_replays_identically}` (no false accept across the B2 adversarial cases); plus PHASE4-B3 positive corpora `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_positive_synthetic.rs::{synthetic_balanced_cert_withdrawal_txs_are_valid, synthetic_positive_verdict_stream_replays_byte_identical}` and the cert/withdrawal-bearing real-corpus coverage in `tx_validity_positive_corpus.rs`, plus the B3 adversarial conservation corpus `crates/ade_ledger/tests/conway_conservation_adversarial.rs::{adversarial_imbalanced_via_deposit, adversarial_imbalanced_via_withdrawal, adversarial_unknown_cert_tag_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_removed_tag_rejects_as_era_invalid, adversarial_truncated_withdrawals_rejects_as_decode, adversarial_state_dependent_unaccountable_rejects, adversarial_no_false_accept, adversarial_verdicts_replay_byte_identical}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`. `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B2", "PHASE4-B3"]`. The no-false-accept property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`, `adversarial_no_false_accept`) and the positive-corpus property (`all_corpus_txs_valid`, `synthetic_balanced_cert_withdrawal_txs_are_valid`) have no dedicated corpus CI gate — proven by the test surface. See §G. |

### `DC-TXV-04`: Total evolution

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD explicit-total-transition doctrine; Cardano ledger spec. PHASE4-B2 new rule. |
| **Requirement** | A `Valid` transaction yields an applied `LedgerState'` (the mempool's accumulating view); an `Invalid` transaction leaves the input state unchanged plus a structured reason. No partial or in-place mutation occurs on the invalid path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/transition.rs` (`tx_validity`: `Valid` -> applied state via `rules::apply_conway_tx_to_utxo`; every `Invalid` path returns `invalid()` which clones the input state unchanged); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/verdict.rs` (closed `TxValidityVerdict`/`TxRejectClass`/`TxValidityError`; total `class()`). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_validity_compose.rs::{valid_tx_is_valid_and_applies, invalid_tx_leaves_state_unchanged, class_mapping_is_total}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (`TxValidityVerdict`/`TxRejectClass`/`TxValidityError` must stay closed structured values). |

### `DC-TXV-05`: Closed era-versioned required-signer enumeration

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (UTXOW required-signers per era); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B2 new rule. **OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY adds `DC-LEDGER-10`** to this rule's `cross_ref` (bidirectional): the required-signer / witness closure resolves certificate and input credentials by discriminated `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}` identity, so the credential-fidelity rule and the signer-closure rule reference each other; `DC-LEDGER-10` lists `DC-TXV-05` back. |
| **Requirement** | For each era, `required_signers(state, tx_body)` is a closed, explicit, era-versioned function over every signer source (resolved input payment credentials, explicit required-signers, certificate key hashes, withdrawal key hashes, Conway governance/voting witnesses, collateral-input implications). A signer source not represented in the era's closed enumeration is impossible to silently omit; incomplete enumeration is a forbidden false-accept path. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs` (closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enum + `required_signers`/`tx_derived_required_signers` grounded in Conway `getConwayWitsVKeyNeeded` + `getVKeyWitnessConwayTxCert`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs` (fail-closed coverage over the preserved body hash); `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs` (`verify_conway_witness_closure` body-path wiring). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/tests/tx_witness_closure.rs::{all_required_covered_is_valid, missing_input_payment_witness_rejected, missing_explicit_required_signer_rejected, missing_withdrawal_witness_rejected, missing_certificate_witness_rejected, missing_governance_voter_witness_rejected, unresolvable_input_is_fail_fast, unresolvable_collateral_input_is_fail_fast, script_credential_input_not_a_vkey_signer, script_credential_certificate_not_a_vkey_signer, collateral_payment_key_is_required, non_conway_era_is_unsupported, closure_is_deterministic}` (within the 20-test `tx_witness_closure` suite covering the 6-source closure hard gates). |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` (`SignerSource` / `RequiredSignerError` / `WitnessClosureError` must stay closed). |

### `DC-TXV-06`: Closed/total Conway certificate-deposit classification

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; UTXO deposit/refund accounting); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine. PHASE4-B3 new rule; CI-enforced in PHASE4-B3F. Cross-refs `T-CONSERV-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-05`, `DC-TXV-07`. |
| **Requirement** | For each era, the certificate-deposit classification `map(state, cert)` is a closed, total, era-versioned function: every certificate variant resolves to exactly one of `new_deposit(coin)` / `refund(coin)` / `neutral` / `explicit_reject`, with the coin sourced from the cert (Conway explicit-deposit variants) or the protocol parameter (legacy variants). An unrecognized cert tag, malformed cert CBOR, or undecodable withdrawals field is a deterministic reject, never a silent neutral. State-dependent cases that cannot be accounted (e.g. pool re-registration charged as a new deposit) reject with a structured `UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting` error rather than guessing. Incomplete classification is a forbidden false-accept path feeding the value-conservation equation. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (`decode_conway_certs`, closed `ConwayCert` grammar — total decode over tags 0..18); `crates/ade_codec/src/error.rs` (`CodecError::UnknownCertTag`; `RemovedInConway` for tags 5/6); `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` (`ConwayCert`, `CertDisposition`, `DepositEffect`, `CoinSource` — closed sum types); `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` (`classify`: compiler-exhaustive `match` mapping every variant to exactly one disposition); `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` (`UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting`); `corpus/conway_certs/{classification_table.md,tags.json}`. |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{decode_total_over_tags_0_18, unknown_cert_tag_is_codec_error, removed_tag_5_6_is_not_valid_in_conway, malformed_cert_cbor_rejected, decode_is_replay_deterministic}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs::tests::{class_mapping_is_total, legacy_unregistration_unresolved_is_unsupported_state_dependent, legacy_unregistration_resolves_recorded_deposit, pool_reregistration_is_neutral, pool_new_registration_charges_pool_deposit}`; plus PHASE4-B3F decoder-strictness regressions `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs::{trailing_bytes_after_cert_array_rejected, huge_array_count_rejects_without_overallocating}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh` — dedicated grep-gate landed in PHASE4-B3F that flips `status = "partial" -> "enforced"`. It fails CI on: (1) `#[non_exhaustive]` or an open-tail `Other`/`Unknown` variant on `ConwayCert` / `CertDisposition` / `DepositEffect` / `CoinSource` in `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs`; (2) a missing `CodecError::UnknownCertTag` reject or a catch-all decoder arm (single-line `_ => …ConwayCert::` or block-form `_ => { … ConwayCert:: … }`) in `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` (the reintroduced-Shelley-fallback anti-pattern); (3) any `_ =>` wildcard arm in `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` (`classify` must stay compiler-exhaustive). Gate **PASSES** at HEAD `193d2fc` (`PASS: Conway cert classification is closed and total (DC-TXV-06)`, exit 0). The closure no longer rests on compiler-exhaustive `match` + tests alone — it is now CI-enforced. _(Residue: `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` is still outside `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` `TARGETS`, but the dedicated gate above covers the closure, so `DC-TXV-06` is genuinely `enforced`.)_ See §A000. |

### `DC-TXV-07`: Canonical deposit-parameter authority

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | IDD determinism doctrine (deposit params are canonical input); Conway protocol-parameter surface. PHASE4-B3 new rule. Cross-refs `T-DET-01`, `T-CONSERV-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-TXV-06`. |
| **Requirement** | All deposit/refund amounts used by Conway transaction value-conservation accounting must be sourced from canonical ledger protocol parameters or explicit certificate fields, never from testkit defaults, shell configuration, ambient `ConwayGovParams`, or fallback constants. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` (`ConwayOnlyDepositParams`, `ConwayDepositParams` — the canonical deposit-param value); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` (`LedgerState.conway_deposit_params` + the `conway_deposit_view` boundary view, which fails fast via `ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingConwayDepositParams` when a Conway state lacks deposit params — see `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs`); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`fingerprint_pparams`, Conway-gated deposit-param fold). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs::tests::{conway_deposit_params_canonical_source, non_conway_state_has_no_conway_deposit_params}`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::tests::{pparams_fingerprint_stable_for_non_conway, pparams_fingerprint_includes_conway_deposits_when_present}`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_deposit_param_authority.sh` (PHASE4-B3 — greps the 6 BLUE crates and FAILs on any non-canonical deposit-param source: testkit `ConwayGovParams` reference in a BLUE path, `ProtocolParameters::default()` feeding `drep_deposit`/`gov_action_deposit`/`key_deposit`/`pool_deposit`, an inline literal assigned to a Conway deposit field outside `conway_deposit_params`, or `env::var` feeding a deposit param). `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B3"]`. |

---

## CN — Classification Table Invariants (`classification_table.md`)

> Most `CN-*` rules remain `status = "declared"` in the registry at HEAD —
> three were flipped `declared → enforced` in `78da6c9` (CN-STORE-03/04/05).
> Five (`CN-CONS-01..05`) were strengthened in PHASE4-N-B by populating
> `code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_script` arrays while still carrying their
> declared/partial status. One (`CN-EPOCH-01`) was flipped
> `declared → partial`. One (`CN-CRYPTO-02`) was flipped
> `declared → partial`. The remaining classification-table entries are
> restatements of `T-*` invariants and inherit enforcement through their
> `cross_ref` targets, but the registry has not yet propagated the
> linkage. Each entry below records the canonical requirement, points
> at the cross-referenced `T-*` / `DC-*` rule where de-facto enforcement
> lives, and flags the registry gap.

### `CN-WIRE-01`: Hash-critical bytes preserved

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A. |
| **Requirement** | Hash-critical original bytes must be preserved and used on all hash/signature-critical paths. |
| **Code** | De-facto via `T-ENC-01` / `DC-CBOR-02` — `crates/ade_codec/src/preserved.rs`. _(Registry direct linkage gap.)_ |
| **Tests** | De-facto via `T-ENC-03` / `DC-CBOR-01`. |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_hash_uses_wire_bytes.sh`. |

### `CN-WIRE-02`: One canonical internal encoding

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A. |
| **Requirement** | Internal replay/state surfaces must use exactly one canonical project encoding. |
| **Code** | De-facto via `T-ENC-01`. _(Registry linkage gap.)_ |
| **Tests** | De-facto via `T-DET-01`. |
| **CI** | _(no CI enforcement — gap)_ |

### `CN-WIRE-03`: Deserialization equivalence across versions

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §A (directly addresses Nov 2025 fork). |

### `CN-CRYPTO-02`: Domain-separated consensus hashes

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | `classification_table.md` §J. |
| **Requirement** | All consensus-relevant hashes must be domain-separated and unambiguous. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/vrf_cert.rs` (PHASE4-N-B S-B3: typed Praos VRF input — 8-byte BE slot ‖ 32-byte epoch nonce ‖ 1-byte role tag, NONCE=0x4E / LEADER=0x4C — built by a single audited function so callers cannot accidentally cross domains). |
| **Tests** | `crates/ade_core/tests/vrf_cert_threshold.rs::{vrf_input_layout_is_41_bytes_with_correct_tag, vrf_role_tags_match_convention, vrf_input_byte_layout}`. |
| **CI** | _(no dedicated CI script — gap; status = `partial`. Strengthened in PHASE4-N-B via the typed-input pattern and test surface; discharged structurally via `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`.)_ Flipped `declared → partial` in PHASE4-N-B. |

## RO — Release Obligations (Project Constitution §4a)

> All `RO-*` rules are release-tier obligations. None have `code_locus`,
> `tests`, or `ci_script` populated in the registry. They are
> release-gate criteria, not HEAD-time enforcement points; this is by
> design and is recorded here as the explicit "no CI at HEAD" state.

## OP — Operational Invariants (Project Constitution §4b)

## Named ingress chokepoint registry (cross-cutting, T-INGRESS-01 / DC-INGRESS-01 / CN-WIRE-06)

The full named-chokepoint list at HEAD `b9ff041`. `ci/ci_check_ingress_chokepoints.sh` enforces that raw CBOR decoding outside `ade_codec` is forbidden except at these named sites; Check 3 currently allowlists exactly the one non-`ade_codec` entry. Adding a new chokepoint requires (a) listing it in the script's header comment, (b) adding the corresponding path to the allowlist if it lives outside `ade_codec`, and (c) updating this table.

| # | Chokepoint | Crate | Surface |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `decode_block_envelope` | `ade_codec` | Era-tagged block envelope |
| 2 | `decode_byron_ebb_block` | `ade_codec` | Byron EBB block CBOR |
| 3 | `decode_byron_regular_block` | `ade_codec` | Byron regular block CBOR |
| 4 | `decode_shelley_block` | `ade_codec` | Shelley block CBOR |
| 5 | `decode_allegra_block` | `ade_codec` | Allegra block CBOR |
| 6 | `decode_mary_block` | `ade_codec` | Mary block CBOR |
| 7 | `decode_alonzo_block` | `ade_codec` | Alonzo block CBOR |
| 8 | `decode_babbage_block` | `ade_codec` | Babbage block CBOR |
| 9 | `decode_conway_block` | `ade_codec` | Conway block CBOR |
| 10 | `decode_address` | `ade_codec` | Address CBOR (Byron/Shelley legacy + Shelley) |
| 11 | `PlutusScript::from_cbor` | `ade_plutus` | Plutus script CBOR (distinct surface from block CBOR; uses aiken/pallas internally) |

The PHASE4-N-B consensus surface does *not* introduce a new named-chokepoint entry — `EraSchedule` enters BLUE consensus as a typed-value parameter built from genesis text in RED (`crates/ade_runtime/src/consensus/genesis_parser.rs`), not as a CBOR-decoded chokepoint, so the chokepoint registry above is unchanged.

---

## Repo-wide CI scripts not yet pinned to a rule

Three CI scripts under `ci/` enforce repo hygiene rather than a single
invariant. They are run on every push but do not appear in any rule's
CI row above:

| Script | What it enforces | Why it is not pinned to a registry rule |
|---|---|---|
| `ci/ci_check_no_secrets.sh` | No credentials, IPs, hostnames, or keys committed to the tree. | Project hygiene rule (per `MEMORY.md::feedback_no_credential_leaks.md`); not an invariant in the project constitution. Candidate for an `OP-SEC-*` entry in a future registry pass. |
| `ci/ci_check_pallas_quarantine.sh` | `pallas-*` references confined to `ade_plutus`. | Phase 2C obligation `O-29.2` (CODEMAP §CI enforcement table) — confines aiken/pallas transitive types to the quarantine crate. Candidate for a `CN-WIRE-*` strengthening or a new `DC-PLUTUS-*` entry. |
| `ci/git-hooks/commit-msg` | Local commit-msg hook rejects commits without `Co-Authored-By: Claude` trailer. | Per-repo IDD scaffolding (HEAD_DELTAS §5 second table). Not a constitution rule. Not applicable to TRACEABILITY as currently scoped. |

---

## Cross-references and consistency warnings

These warnings are surfaced for the parent's downstream review; they do
not block doc generation.

### A000000000000. PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE close — 1 NEW rule (`DC-LEDGER-11`), 1 new CI script, 1 new canonical type (`ProposalProcedure`); bidirectional `DC-LEDGER-10 ↔ DC-LEDGER-11`; all 6 CE-PP-* green in CI; cluster archived

Cluster PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE (closure of the Conway `proposal_procedures`
opacity at the tx-body boundary, 2 slices `70bc85b` PP-S1 → `928c2be` PP-S2) is now
**fully closed at HEAD `928c2be`**. The registry total moves to **176 rules** at HEAD
`928c2be` (+1 from `DC-LEDGER-11`); the CI count moves to **32 scripts plus one git
hook** (+1 from `ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh`). This is the first
cluster since OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY to both add a new registry rule **and** add a
new CI script; every prior cluster since OQ5 only strengthened an existing rule and
extended the existing `ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` gate. **All six
CE-PP-* mechanical acceptance criteria are mechanically green in CI** at HEAD
`928c2be` — there is no deferred half (unlike PHASE4-N-E's CE-N-E-7 deferral to
CE-NODE-N2C-LTX).

**New rule (`DC-LEDGER-11` within DC):**

| Rule | Status | Code authority | Discharging CI |
|---|---|---|---|
| `DC-LEDGER-11` | **enforced** (PROPOSAL-PROCEDURES-DECODE) | `ade_codec::conway::governance` (`decode_proposal_procedures` single closed entry point + `decode_proposal_procedure` per-procedure 4-tuple + `decode_gov_action` closed dispatch + `encode_proposal_procedures` byte-identical round-trip) + `ade_types::conway::governance` (`ProposalProcedure` closed struct) + `ade_codec::conway::tx` (typed key 20 path on `ConwayTxBody`) + GREEN `ade_testkit::governance::proposal_procedures_replay` (PP-S2 canonical synthetic corpus + replay harness, exercising every `GovAction` variant + the `UpdateCommittee` discriminant case) + **21 tests** (14 unit in PP-S1 inline `mod tests` + 3 integration in PP-S1 `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_tx_body_proposal_procedures.rs` + 4 corpus in PP-S2 `crates/ade_testkit/tests/proposal_procedures_corpus_replay.rs`) | `ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` (new, 5-check mechanical guard) + `ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (bidirectional cross_ref) |

**Bidirectional pairing (NO strengthening of any existing rule's `strengthened_in`; `cross_ref`-only):**

| Target rule | Relationship | Why |
|---|---|---|
| `DC-LEDGER-10` | structural pairing | The new typed `proposal_procedures` decode reuses the existing closed `GovAction` enum. Its `UpdateCommittee` arm carries the structured `{removed, added, threshold}` with `StakeCredential` cold members (the ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK shape), so PP-S1 cannot re-collapse the committee-credential discriminant that `DC-LEDGER-10` defends. `DC-LEDGER-10.cross_ref` gains `DC-LEDGER-11`; `DC-LEDGER-11.cross_ref = ["DC-LEDGER-10"]`. Bidirectional. |

**Type / shape changes shipped by PP-S1 (`70bc85b`):**

| Item | Before | After | Where |
|---|---|---|---|
| `ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` field type | `Option<Vec<u8>>` (opaque CBOR pass-through) | `Option<Vec<ProposalProcedure>>` (closed typed grammar) | `crates/ade_types/src/conway/tx.rs` |
| `ConwayTxBody` key 20 codec path | `data[start..end].to_vec()` opaque pass-through | typed `decode_proposal_procedures` / `encode_proposal_procedures` | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/tx.rs` |
| New closed struct | _absent_ | `ProposalProcedure { deposit: Coin, return_addr: <bytes>, gov_action: GovAction, anchor: Anchor }` | `crates/ade_types/src/conway/governance.rs` |
| New codec module | _absent_ | `ade_codec::conway::governance` (exports `decode_proposal_procedures`, `decode_proposal_procedure`, `decode_gov_action`, `encode_proposal_procedures`) | `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/governance.rs` |
| Test-file cleanup per OQ-8 | ~10 test files referenced `Some(vec![0x80])` opaque placeholder | converted to `None` where they did not need actual proposal-procedure data | various `crates/*/tests/` |

Only two of the test-file references actually needed an update; the rest already
used `None`. The cleanup is a strict tightening, not a behavioural change.

| Item | Path | What it does |

**New CI script (PP-S1, anchored on `DC-LEDGER-11`):**

`ci/ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` defends the closure mechanically with
five checks (see the `DC-LEDGER-11` CI row above for the precise enumeration):
(1) closed `ProposalProcedure` struct + 4-field shape; (2) typed
`ConwayTxBody.proposal_procedures` field (not `Option<Vec<u8>>`); (3)
`ade_codec::conway::governance` exports the typed decoder + encoder; (4) the
key-20 path on `ConwayTxBody` uses the typed decoder/encoder, never the opaque
pass-through; (5) no production `ProposalProcedure {` struct-literal construction
outside the sanctioned synthesis sites (production callers MUST go through
`decode_proposal_procedures`). Test code (`crates/*/tests/`, `#[cfg(test)] mod
tests` blocks) and the GREEN harness under `ade_testkit/` are exempt by design.

| CE-PP-3 | Single closed entry point + closed `GovAction` dispatch | `ci_check_proposal_procedures_closed.sh` check 3/5 + `decode_proposal_procedures` + `decode_gov_action` in `ade_codec::conway::governance` |

**OPEN OBLIGATIONS (recorded on `DC-LEDGER-11.open_obligation`, NOT mechanical gaps;
deferred by cluster scope decisions, NOT regressions):**

- **OQ-1 — `voting_procedures` (tx body key 19) closure.** The natural sibling
  cluster: same opaque-bytes shape, same pressure, deliberately deferred. This
  rule does **NOT** cover key 19; a future cluster (`VOTING-PROCEDURES-DECODE` or
  similar) is the recommended next discriminant work.
- **OQ-2 — `ParameterChange.update` nested opacity.** `ParameterChange` is a
  closed `GovAction` arm at PP-S1, but its inner `update` payload remains opaque
  bytes (the protocol-parameter-update sub-grammar is its own future closure
  decision). A future `strengthened_in += <ppupdate-cluster>` candidate.
- **OQ-3 — `NewConstitution.raw` nested opacity.** Same shape as OQ-2: the arm
  is closed at PP-S1, the inner `raw` payload is opaque bytes; a future
  `strengthened_in` candidate when that sub-grammar is closed.
- **OQ-4 — Typed `RewardAccount` for `proposal_procedure.return_addr`.** A
  separate fidelity decision — `return_addr` is currently bytes (`RewardAccount`
  as encoded); typing it (`Network` + `StakeCredential`) is a separate cluster.

None of these are mechanical CI gaps in this cluster's scope — the gates discharge
exactly what `DC-LEDGER-11` was scoped to defend (the outer `proposal_procedures`
list + each procedure's 4-tuple + the closed `GovAction` dispatch). The nested
opacities are scoped to future siblings by explicit OQ resolution.

1. **`DC-TXV-06` is now `status = "enforced"`** with `ci_script = ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh` (PHASE4-B3F) — the gate's non-empty-`ci_script`-on-`enforced` requirement is satisfied.
2. **`DC-TXV-06` and `DC-TXV-07` carry `cluster = "CL-LEDGER-VERDICT"`**, which is in the gate's allowed cluster set.
3. **`DC-TXV-06` is now `status = "enforced"`** with a non-empty `ci_script` (`ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh`); the gate's `enforced`-entry requirement is satisfied.
4. **Cross_refs are bidirectional.** `DC-TXV-06`/`DC-TXV-07` reference `T-CONSERV-01`, `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-05`, `T-DET-01`, and each other; those target rules list `DC-TXV-06`/`DC-TXV-07` back in their `cross_ref` arrays (verified in `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml`).

With PHASE4-B3F the DC-TXV-06 CI grep-gate is **landed and CLOSED** — `status = "enforced"` is now the correct classification. There is **no remaining enforcement gap** in the B3/B3F cert-classification + value-conservation surface; every B3/B3F rule (`DC-TXV-06`, `DC-TXV-07`, `T-CONSERV-01`, `DC-VAL-06`, `DC-TXV-03`) carries a discharging CI script.

**Status:** cluster work closed; PHASE4-B3F follow-up closed; **constitution-coverage gate PASSES**. The DC-TXV-06 CI grep-gate is **landed (no longer a follow-up)**. CE-B3/B3F enforcement evidence reproducible via `cargo test -p ade_ledger --test conway_conservation_full --test conway_conservation_adversarial --test conway_conservation_positive_synthetic`, `cargo test -p ade_codec --test conway_cert_classification`, `cargo test -p ade_ledger cert_classify::tests pparams::tests fingerprint::tests`, `bash ci/ci_check_deposit_param_authority.sh`, `bash ci/ci_check_conway_cert_classification_closed.sh` (PASS, exit 0), and `bash ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` (PASS, 170 entries, exits 0).

**Documented deposit/refund value-conservation gap (known gap; see §H):**
PHASE4-B2-S4 found and fixed a real fail-open — the Conway state-backed path never checked coin-level value conservation, so `outputs + fee != inputs` was accepted as `Valid` at `track_utxo=true`. The fix (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation`) enforces `sum(inputs) == sum(outputs) + fee + donation` for **cert/withdrawal-free** txs. Full preservation-of-value with deposit/refund/withdrawal accounting is **deferred**: the check conservatively skips txs carrying certificates or withdrawals (so it never false-rejects), which means a mis-accounted deposit/refund/withdrawal tx is not yet caught on value grounds. This is a tx-validity-completeness item against `T-CONSERV-01` / `CN-LEDGER-07`. Recorded in `MEMORY.md::project_value_conservation_deposits_deferred.md` and in `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs`. Surfaced in §G and §H.

**Status:** closed. CE-B2 evidence reproducible via
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test tx_witness_closure`,
`--test tx_validity_compose`,
`--test tx_validity_positive_corpus`,
`--test tx_validity_adversarial_corpus`,
`--test mempool_admission`; `ci/ci_check_constitution_coverage.sh` PASSES (168 entries).

| `CN-EPOCH-01` | partial (strengthened); `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-N-B", "PHASE4-B1"]` | added ledger-side `consensus_view.rs` epoch-projection + `consensus_view` tests |

**Documented Conway body-witness verification gap (known gap, fenced; to close in B2):**
The adversarial corpus mutator M6 (forge a witness, then patch the header `body_hash`
to the mutated body) lands fail-closed at `HeaderInvalid` (KES) because the KES
signature signs the header body — which includes `body_hash` — and the header
pipeline runs before the body authority. So a forged spend cannot pass
`block_validity` by any byte mutation of a real block. **However**, when the inner
block is fed *directly* to `ade_ledger::rules::apply_block_with_verdicts` for a
Conway block (bypassing the header, which a real chain never does), the fabricated
vkey witness is **not** rejected — the Conway body authority runs structural +
Plutus dispatch without per-tx Ed25519 vkey-witness verification. This is **not
reachable through `block_validity`** (the header fences it), so it is not a CE-B1-4
false-accept, but it is a genuine pre-release finding against the witness-verification
invariant (`DC-LEDGER-05` / `CN-LEDGER-09`). Recorded in
`crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs` (M6 doc comment) and
`corpus/validity/adversarial/README.md` (§ "Separate, deeper note"). **Scheduled for
B2 (tx validity).** Not double-recorded as a registry gap because it lives outside the
`block_validity` authority surface B1 closed; surfaced here in §G.

**Discrepancy note (prompt vs registry):** the close summary listed `T-ENC-01` among
the PHASE4-B1 strengthenings, but the registry `T-ENC-01` entry carries no
`PHASE4-B1` in `strengthened_in` (it remains `status = "partial"` with no
`strengthened_in` field). No change was made to the `T-ENC-01` rule entry above. See §G #6.

**Status:** closed. CE-B1 evidence reproducible via
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test block_validity_compose`,
`--test block_validity_positive_corpus`, `--test block_validity_adversarial_corpus`,
`cargo test -p ade_core --test praos_header_validate`,
`cargo test -p ade_ledger --test consensus_view`.

### B. `DC-STORE-04` Tier 5 divergence (documented, not a gap)

`DC-STORE-04` literally describes cardano-node's three-DB architecture
(ImmutableDB + VolatileDB + LedgerDB). Ade has deliberately diverged
per CE-79 Tier 5 (intentional-divergence on non-hash-critical
operator-facing surfaces, per `MEMORY.md::feedback_diverge_on_internal_surfaces.md`):
a single redb-backed store with logical separation via key prefixes
(`slots_by_hash`, `hashes_by_slot`, `snapshots_by_slot`) under
`crates/ade_runtime/src/chaindb/persistent.rs`.

The **semantic guarantees** that DC-STORE-04 was designed to deliver —
append-only finalized data and atomic snapshots — survive in Ade and
are now mechanically enforced under `DC-STORE-02` and `DC-STORE-03`
respectively, both flipped `declared → enforced` in `78da6c9`. The rule
remains `status = "declared"` in the registry rather than `enforced`
because Ade does not implement the literal three-DB topology DC-STORE-04
names; per IDD discipline, rules are append-only and may only be
strengthened, not weakened or repointed. A future `DC-STORE-04A`
strengthening (or a deprecation event paired with a major version bump)
is the legal way to reclassify.

This is recorded in the registry as a comment block above the
`DC-STORE-04` entry (commit `78da6c9`), in the `DC-STORE-04` row above,
and here in §B. **It does not read as an enforcement gap.** It is a
documented Tier 5 divergence with the semantic guarantee preserved
elsewhere and mechanically enforced.

- `crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/` — 5 modules (BLUE): `mod.rs`, `verdict.rs` (closed `Valid`/`Invalid` + `FieldKind`/`FieldError` taxonomy), `transition.rs` (header ∧ body composition; total state evolution), `header_input.rs` (body-hash binding), `encoding.rs`.

- `crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs` — extended for B1 (`expect_size` fail-closed guard + VRF-keyhash binding + KES authentication). The CODEMAP `ade_core::consensus` row above lists 16 modules; `kes_check.rs` is the 17th and is not yet enumerated.
- `crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/` — 5 GREEN modules: `mod.rs`, `corpus.rs`, `ledger_view.rs`, `replay.rs` (positive-corpus harness), `adversarial.rs` (M1–M6 mutators).
- New test files: `crates/ade_ledger/tests/{block_validity_compose,block_validity_positive_corpus,block_validity_adversarial_corpus,consensus_view}.rs`; `crates/ade_core/tests/praos_header_validate.rs`.

**PHASE4-B2 additions not yet enumerated in CODEMAP, SEAMS, or HEAD_DELTAS:**
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/` — 7 BLUE modules: `mod.rs`, `verdict.rs` (closed `TxValidityVerdict`/`TxRejectClass`/`TxValidityError`), `transition.rs` (phase-1 ∧ phase-2 composition; total state evolution), `phase1.rs` (decode + state-backed checks), `required_signers.rs` (closed era-versioned `SignerSource` enumeration), `witness.rs` (fail-closed Ed25519 coverage over the preserved body hash), `encoding.rs`.
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/` — 3 BLUE modules: `mod.rs`, `admit.rs` (closed `AdmitOutcome`; admission == `tx_validity`), `policy.rs` (closed `OrderPolicy`; deterministic shedding).
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` — new coin-conservation check (PHASE4-B2-S4); conservative scope (see §H).
- `crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/` — GREEN modules: `mod.rs`, `extract.rs`, `valid_synthetic.rs`, `adversarial.rs` (tx positive/adversarial corpus harness).
- New test files: `crates/ade_ledger/tests/{tx_witness_closure,tx_validity_compose,tx_validity_positive_corpus,tx_validity_adversarial_corpus,mempool_admission}.rs`.

**PHASE4-N-E additions not yet enumerated in CODEMAP (CODEMAP is being regenerated in parallel with this refresh; expected to catch up to HEAD `43fcc31`):**
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/ingress.rs` — BLUE: closed `IngressEvent` / `IngressSource` types and the `mempool_ingress` single sanctioned production bridge into `admit`.
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/canonicalize.rs` — BLUE: deterministic canonical-order canonicalizer that round-robins per-peer `PeerSubmissionQueue`s by sorted `PeerId`, preserving tx bytes verbatim and propagating the source from the queue.
- `crates/ade_testkit/src/mempool/ingress_replay.rs` — GREEN harness: `wrap_as_ingress`, `b_track_corpus_as_ingress`, `replay_ingress_trace`, `BTrackCase`, `ExpectedOutcome`. The harness goes through `mempool_ingress` (the BLUE bridge), never through `admit` directly.
- New test files: `crates/ade_ledger/tests/mempool_ingress.rs` (6 tests); `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_replay.rs` (5 tests); `crates/ade_testkit/tests/mempool_ingress_canonicalize.rs` (2 tests). Inline test growth in `crates/ade_ledger/src/mempool/{ingress,canonicalize}.rs`.

**PHASE4-B3 additions (CODEMAP regenerated at HEAD `193d2fc` — these should now be present; verify on the next read):**
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs` — BLUE module: closed/total Conway certificate-deposit classification (`classify`, compiler-exhaustive `match`).
- `crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs` — BLUE: `decode_conway_certs` + closed `ConwayCert` grammar; `crates/ade_codec/src/error.rs` adds `CodecError::UnknownCertTag` / `RemovedInConway`.
- `crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs` — BLUE: closed `ConwayCert` / `CertDisposition` / `DepositEffect` / `CoinSource` sum types.
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/pparams.rs` — BLUE: `ConwayOnlyDepositParams` / `ConwayDepositParams` (canonical deposit-param value); `crates/ade_ledger/src/state.rs` gains `conway_deposit_params` + `conway_deposit_view`; `crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs` gains `ValidationEnvironmentError::MissingConwayDepositParams`.
- `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation` — full preservation-of-value equation (early-out removed); `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs::fingerprint_pparams` Conway-gated deposit fold.
- New test files: `crates/ade_ledger/tests/{conway_conservation_full,conway_conservation_adversarial,conway_conservation_positive_synthetic}.rs`; `crates/ade_codec/tests/conway_cert_classification.rs`. New corpus: `corpus/conway_certs/{classification_table.md,tags.json}`.

The CODEMAP regenerated at HEAD `193d2fc` (per the close brief) should carry these modules. Earlier baselines listed `block_validity` but **no `tx_validity`, `mempool`, or `cert_classify`** — confirm the fresh CODEMAP picks up the full B2 + B3 BLUE authority surface.

CODEMAP refresh is required to pick up these modules and to update the
CI-script count (19 → 25; +4 PHASE4-N-B + 2 PHASE4-N-A counted in the
prior refresh). The next `/codemap` regeneration will resolve this.
This is a known doc-version skew, not a code drift.

### E. HEAD_DELTAS §5 cross-check

`ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`, `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`,
`ci_check_no_density_in_fork_choice.sh`. This is a known doc skew —
HEAD_DELTAS is regenerated on phase boundaries (per
`.idd-config.json::head_deltas_baseline` doctrine), and the next
`/head-deltas` run will pick them up. PHASE4-B1 **added no CI script**, so §5
has no missing-script skew from B1; but HEAD_DELTAS does not yet narrate the
`block_validity` authority surface or the `DC-VAL-*` rules — same regen-on-phase-boundary skew.

and populated previously-empty `ci_script` fields), so §5 has no missing-script skew from B2;
but the §5 row for `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` still describes only the B1 extension
(`ade_core/src/consensus/` + `ade_ledger/src/block_validity/`) and does not yet reflect the B2
extension to `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/` + `ade_ledger/src/mempool/`. HEAD_DELTAS also does
not yet narrate the `tx_validity` / `mempool` authority surface or the `DC-TXV-*` / `DC-MEM-*`
rules — same regen-on-phase-boundary skew. The next `/head-deltas` run resolves both.

as `candidate` / `proposed` future attach points — both are now *realized* in `ade_ledger`

### G. Open questions for the user

1. **`DC-CONS-09` and `DC-CONS-10` have no dedicated CI script.** Both
   are marked `status = "enforced"` via test surface only. Worth
   considering whether (a) the existing `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`
   already discharges them structurally (current implicit answer), or
   (b) a new narrow CI script — e.g. a corpus replay gate — should be
   added. No action taken in this refresh.
2. **`DC-CONSENSUS-02` registry status is `partial` with empty `ci_script`.**
   The leader-schedule corpus tests + structural CIs discharge it
   de-facto, but no dedicated `ci/ci_check_leader_schedule.sh` exists.
   Recommend adding one or accepting the de-facto discharge.
3. **`CN-CONS-04` (header/body binding) `code_locus` and `tests`
   populated but `ci_script` empty.** Same de-facto pattern as above —
   `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` keeps `HeaderValidationError`
   closed but no dedicated header-validate CI exists.
4. **CN-EPOCH-01 newly flipped to `partial`** with consensus-side
   evidence; ledger-side `epoch.rs`/`governance.rs` evidence also
   exists via `DC-LEDGER-04`. Consider unifying under a single CI gate
   or accepting the split.
5. **`ade_core` CODEMAP entry needs a substantial rewrite** — the
   "empty placeholder" classification is no longer accurate (16 BLUE
   consensus modules under `src/consensus/`, +`kes_check.rs` from B1). The
   next `/codemap` refresh will fix this, but the gap is worth flagging now.
6. **All six `DC-VAL-*` rules are `status = "enforced"` with empty
   `ci_script`.** They are proven by their test surface (positive +
   adversarial corpora, compose tests) and discharged structurally by
   `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` / `ci_check_forbidden_patterns.sh` /
   `ci_check_no_float_in_consensus.sh`, but **no dedicated
   `ci/ci_check_block_validity.sh` exists**. The CE-B1-4 no-false-accept
   property (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) and the 14/14 positive-corpus
   property (`all_corpus_blocks_valid`) currently have no CI gate. Recommend
   a single block-validity corpus CI gate, or accept the de-facto discharge.
7. **`DC-VAL-06`'s fail-open-pattern ban is not text-scanned.** The rule
   forbids `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` in BLUE validation, but
   no CI script greps for that pattern — it is proven only by the adversarial
   corpus. Strong candidate for a new `ci/ci_check_no_fail_open_len_guard.sh`.
8. **Conway body-witness verification gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B2-S1 (CE-B2-1).**
   Previously: the Conway body authority did not perform per-tx Ed25519
   vkey-witness verification when reached directly (bypassing the header). Now
   wired into the body path via
   `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs::verify_required_witnesses`
   (L78) — called from `crates/ade_ledger/src/rules.rs:258` and `:342` through
   `verify_conway_witness_closure` — with the closed era-versioned `SignerSource`
   enumeration in `crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs`
   covering every signer source (resolved inputs, explicit required-signers,
   cert/withdrawal/voter/collateral). Discharged by `DC-LEDGER-05` /
   `CN-LEDGER-09` / `DC-TXV-05` (all carry `strengthened_in += PHASE4-B2`),
   the 20-test `tx_witness_closure` suite, and `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh`
   over `ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/`. **CLOSED — no further action.**
9. **`T-ENC-01` strengthening discrepancy.** The PHASE4-B1 close summary
   named `T-ENC-01` as strengthened, but the registry entry shows no
   `PHASE4-B1` in `strengthened_in` and remains `partial`. Either the
   registry needs `strengthened_in += ["PHASE4-B1"]` (if B1 genuinely touched
   the canonical-encoding surface) or the close summary overstated. No edit
   was made to the `T-ENC-01` rule entry pending user judgment.
   **Resolved by PHASE4-B2:** the registry now carries `strengthened_in =
   ["PHASE4-B1", "PHASE4-B2"]` on `T-ENC-01` and a non-empty B1/B2 `code_locus`,
   so the discrepancy is closed — B1/B2 genuinely touched the canonical-encoding
   surface (block body hash; `tx_id` over preserved bytes). The rule remains
   `partial` (canonical-encoding coverage incomplete), not a regression.
10. **Deposit/refund value-conservation gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B3-S4.**
    Previously: the Conway coin-conservation check
    (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs::check_conway_coin_conservation`)
    conservatively skipped txs carrying certificates or withdrawals, so a
    mis-accounted deposit/refund/withdrawal tx was not rejected on value
    grounds. The early-out is **gone**: the source comment at the function
    header (L164–166) records "PHASE4-B3-S4 removed the deposit/withdrawal
    early-out that was the cluster's known false-accept path", and the full
    Conway preservation-of-value equation
    (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee + donation + new_deposits`)
    now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs with deposit amounts
    sourced canonically via `DC-TXV-06` / `DC-TXV-07`. Proven by
    `conway_conservation_full`, `conservation_early_out_removed`, the
    adversarial conservation corpus, and the positive corpora (real + synthetic);
    discharged on `T-CONSERV-01` (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B3`),
    `CN-LEDGER-07`, `DC-VAL-06` (`strengthened_in += PHASE4-B3, PHASE4-B3F`).
    See §H (kept for historical provenance). **CLOSED — no further action.**
11. **All five `DC-TXV-*` rules and both `DC-MEM-*` rules share one CI script.**
    `ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` discharges them structurally (closed
    verdict / signer-source / admission taxonomies) but there is **no dedicated
    tx-validity corpus CI gate** — the no-false-accept property
    (`no_mutation_is_ever_valid`) and the 103/103 positive-corpus property
    (`all_corpus_txs_valid`) are proven by the test surface only. Recommend a
    single tx-validity corpus CI gate, or accept the de-facto discharge (mirrors
    the §G #6 / #7 block-validity situation).
12. **`DC-TXV-03` positive corpus runs at `track_utxo=false` (partial scope).**
    The positive/adversarial corpus harness exercises structural + witness
    closure but defers UTxO-dependent checks (the corpus blocks' consumed UTxOs
    are not all resolvable from the committed snapshot). Confirm whether closing
    the UTxO-resolved scope is a future-cluster obligation.
13. **`DC-LEDGER-05` and `CN-LEDGER-09` remain `partial` with no dedicated CI.**
    The Conway witness-closure surface is now real and tested, but the
    era-specific witness binding is discharged only structurally
    (`ci_check_consensus_closed_enums.sh` keeps the taxonomy closed). Consider a
    dedicated witness-binding CI gate.

    re-extracted), or accepted as an environment-blocked open obligation. This is the

21. **OQ-5 — credential key/script discriminant collapse — RESOLVED in OQ5-CREDENTIAL-FIDELITY.**
    The B5-declared OQ-5 follow-up has graduated into the enforced rule `DC-LEDGER-10`:
    `StakeCredential` is now the closed sum `{KeyHash, ScriptHash}`, both era decoders
    preserve the tag (unknown rejects), `CertState`/`ConwayGovState` key on the
    discriminated credential, and `fingerprint::write_stake_credential` serializes the
    discriminant. CI-guarded by `ci/ci_check_credential_discriminant_closed.sh` (PASSES
    at HEAD `a3ee2da`). What remains is a real-chain oracle (environment-blocked, §G #23)
    plus declared non-goals (committee member/vote discrimination; the `Hash28`-keyed
    stake-distribution snapshot; the Byron credential surface) — bounded scope items,
    not the collapse itself. **CLOSED.** Original B5 framing follows for the record:
    **OQ-5 — credential key/script discriminant collapse in `ConwayGovState` keys
    (pre-existing decoder behaviour, newly promoted to authority by B5).** `ConwayGovState`
    keys gov state on bare `Hash28`; the codec `ade_codec` `decode_stake_credential` drops
    the credential type tag, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing the same 28
    bytes are indistinguishable in `vote_delegations` / `committee_hot_keys` / `drep_expiry`.
    cardano-node keys on the full discriminated `Credential`. This is NOT introduced by B5
    — it is pre-existing decoder behaviour that B5 newly promotes into governance authority.
    The 28-byte collision is not cheaply forgeable; carrying the discriminant into
    `StakeCredential`/`DRep` is a separate cross-cutting follow-up touching the whole
    credential surface, tracked per the per-cluster security review. Confirm whether OQ-5
    is carried as a future cross-cutting credential-discriminant cluster.

## H. Value-conservation completeness gap — CLOSED in PHASE4-B3 (tracked against T-CONSERV-01 / CN-LEDGER-07)

> **Status (HEAD `168ac02`, refresh):** **CLOSED** — kept as a historical
> provenance entry only. This refresh removes the gap's two carry-forward
> paragraphs from the PHASE4-B2 / PHASE4-B1 close summaries above (no
> back-reference from the live-code narrative); §G #10 is reclassified
> CLOSED with explicit code citation. The cert/withdrawal early-out was
> removed from `check_conway_coin_conservation` in PHASE4-B3-S4 (source
> comment at `crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs:164-166` explicitly records
> "PHASE4-B3-S4 removed the deposit/withdrawal early-out that was the
> cluster's known false-accept path"); the **full** Conway preservation-of-
> value equation (`Σ(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == Σ(outputs) + fee +
> donation + new_deposits`) now runs for cert/withdrawal-bearing Conway txs,
> with deposit/refund amounts sourced canonically (`DC-TXV-06` closed/total
> cert-deposit classification + `DC-TXV-07` canonical deposit-param
> authority). Proven by `conway_conservation_full`,
> `conservation_early_out_removed`, the adversarial conservation corpus
> (`adversarial_imbalanced_via_{deposit,withdrawal}`,
> `adversarial_no_false_accept`), and the positive corpora (real + synthetic).
> The historical description below is retained for provenance only.

PHASE4-B2-S4 (`crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs`) fixed a real fail-open and
introduced `check_conway_coin_conservation`, which enforces
`sum(inputs) == sum(outputs) + fee + donation` for **certificate- and
withdrawal-free** Conway transactions. This closes the pure-spend
value-conservation hole the tx adversarial corpus surfaced (a tx with
`outputs + fee != inputs` was previously accepted as `Valid` at `track_utxo=true`).

**Still deferred:** full preservation-of-value accounting —
`sum(inputs) + withdrawals + refunds == sum(outputs) + fee + deposits + donation`.
The current check **conservatively skips** txs that carry certificates or
withdrawals (so it can never false-*reject* them), which means a mis-accounted
deposit/refund/withdrawal tx is not yet caught on value grounds. Other checks
may still reject such a tx, but value conservation specifically would not.

This is the one **known, documented tx-validity-completeness gap** against the
value-preservation invariant (`T-CONSERV-01` — UTxO/asset conservation; mirrored
in the declared `CN-LEDGER-07`). It is **not** a silent gap: it is recorded in
`MEMORY.md::project_value_conservation_deposits_deferred.md` and in the
`conway.rs` source comment, and surfaced here and in §G #10. It does **not**
read as a `DC-TXV-*` enforcement gap (those rules close the verdict/witness/total-
evolution surface, all `enforced`) — it is a completeness boundary on the
value-conservation half of phase-1, scoped conservatively so it never
false-rejects.

This doc is purely **rule → enforcement**.

Every `_(no enforcement found — gap)_` line corresponds to a registry
`code_locus`/`tests`/`ci_script` field that is empty for an entry whose
`status` is `declared`, `partial`, or where a cross-referenced rule is
itself a gap. Closing a gap means populating the registry; the next
TRACEABILITY regeneration will lift the gap automatically.

`DC-STORE-04`'s rows are intentionally **not** marked gaps — see §B for
the documented Tier 5 divergence rationale.
